National News Two

110th Meeting of the Legislative Yuan

The Legislative Yuan held its 110th meeting at 9:00 AM on the 20th, with 32 members in attendance, including Jiao Yitang. The meeting was chaired by Hu Hanmin. The matters for discussion were as follows: 1. Deliberation of the Sino-US Arbitration Treaty: It was decided to refer it to the Foreign Affairs Committee for review. 2. The Autonomy Law Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan reported on the review of the Executive Yuan's consultation on whether the provision of Article 54 of the Municipal Organization Law that the district chief is an unpaid position refers specifically to elected district chiefs, and whether appointed district chiefs should be paid before district chiefs are elected. It was decided to pass the review report. The provision of Article 54 of the Municipal Organization Law refers specifically to elected district chiefs. As for the salary of appointed district chiefs, it should be decided by the appointing authority. 3. The Labor Law Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan reported on the review of the Seamen's Union Organization Regulations and the Private Ship Seamen's Union Organization Regulations. It was decided to pass the review report. The Seamen's Union Organization Regulations and the Private Ship Seamen's Union Organization Regulations can be formulated by the competent authorities within the legal scope of the Implementation Law of the Labor Union Law and in accordance with the Outline for Reorganizing Seamen's Unions. There is no need to specify regulations to be handled by legislative procedures. 4. The Labor Law Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan reported on the review of the Executive Yuan's consultation on whether the Labor Arbitration Regulations should be explicitly abolished or supplemented and revised separately based on the request of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. It was decided to pass the review report. The Labor Arbitration Regulations should be submitted to the National Government for explicit abolition and should not be revised or supplemented again. 5. The Legal System Committee of the Legislative Yuan, together with the Military Affairs Committee and the Commercial Law Drafting Committee, reported on the review of the Ship Registration Law draft. It was decided to refer it back to the original review committee, together with the Maritime Law Drafting Committee, for re-examination. 6. The Legal System Committee of the Legislative Yuan, together with the Military Affairs Committee and the Commercial Law Drafting Committee, reported on the review of the Ship Law draft. It was decided to refer it back to the original review committee, together with the Maritime Law Drafting Committee, for re-examination. 7. Deliberation of the International Telegraph Business Regulations: It was decided to refer it to the Foreign Affairs Committee for review. 8. The Military Affairs Committee of the Legislative Yuan reported on the review of the Fortress Zone Law draft. It was decided to refer it back to the Military Affairs Committee, together with Luo Ding, Jiao Yitang, and Sun Jingya, for re-examination.

Executive Yuan Orders Grain Storage in Various Places

The Executive Yuan, in order to store grain, specially instructed the Ministry of Interior and the governments of various provinces, saying: "According to a letter from the Central Political Conference, the 242nd meeting of this conference approved the proposal of Committee Member Guo Fu, who stated that this year's harvest in various places seems to have a surplus of grain. However, based on last year's depleted reserves, there may still be a shortage of grain next year. Currently, during the harvest season, farmers often have to sell grain cheaply due to other consumption or the need to repay debts. Therefore, the recent drop in grain prices is not beneficial to farmers and provides an opportunity for unscrupulous merchants to hoard and speculate. In order to maintain people's food supply, it is appropriate to take advantage of this year's bumper harvest to plan for storage and famine relief. Grain storage warehouses in various places should be set up immediately, and those that already exist should be expanded. The amount of grain to be stored in each county should be promptly determined by the provincial governments according to local conditions. If counties lack funds, they may be allowed to borrow from the financial sector at interest, using the stored grain as collateral. A committee of local impartial people should be organized to be responsible for supervision. In areas where farmers' banks have been established, the farmers' banks should provide farmers with mortgage loans for rice and wheat. In areas where farmers' banks have not been established, various pawnshops should provide mortgage loans for rice and wheat within the interest rate range set by the central government. At the same time, hoarding by merchants should be prohibited, and the export of rice and grain should be strictly prohibited. In this way, farmers will have the opportunity to turn around their finances and will not suffer unnecessary losses in the short term. The grain situation in various places can also be kept in balance. Is this feasible? Please make a public decision." After discussion, it was referred to the Executive Yuan for appropriate recording and transmittal, and it is hoped that it will be checked and handled accordingly. This was received. It was previously reported that the Ministry of Interior had submitted the draft of the Various Local Warehouse Management Regulations, which had been approved by this Yuan and submitted to the National Government for instructions for record. The Ministry was instructed to approve the record for the Ministry to announce. Now, the aforementioned case has been submitted, and it should be handled accordingly. In addition to notifying the governments of the various provinces to comply and ordering the Ministry of Interior to supervise the implementation and report to the National Government for review and also communicate to the Secretariat of the Central Political Conference for reference and transmittal, we are also ordering you to comply and report for our review.

The Min Army Punishing Lu is Advancing Rapidly

Mobilization Order Issued on the 15th

Fuzhou Correspondence: Chen Rongbiao, Brigade Commander of Lu Xingbang's department, recently had an internal conflict with Qian Yuguang, Regiment Commander, in Gutian. Qian then lured and killed Chen. It is now found that although Qian's killing of Chen was due to long-standing grudges, he also received a secret order from Lu Xingrong beforehand. Unexpectedly, after Chen was killed, the troops of Chen's department stationed in Gutian and Dahu gathered at Shuikou, cutting off the traffic between Yanping, Youxi, Dahu, and Gutian, claiming that they would not retreat unless Qian Yuguang was punished. Because Lu's troops' connection with Minbei and Fuzhou was cut off, in order to perfunctorily appease the scattered soldiers and maintain the overall situation, he had no choice but to order Qian to be dismissed and await investigation, and ordered Chen's scattered troops to be incorporated into Lu Xingrong's command. Qian Yuguang, feeling indignant that he was acting on a secret order when he killed Chen, and now he is being blamed, sent representatives to the province to express his sincerity and willingness to lead the troops forward. The authorities, observing his sincerity, approved his request and gave him the title of Commander of the Provisional Provincial Defense Army First Brigade. Qian immediately sent a telegram to defect. At the same time, the provincial side received a telegram from Fang Shengtong, reporting that Dehua had been captured on the 13th and he is currently leading various armies to advance towards Datian, directly approaching Youxi. He requested that the provincial side also quickly send troops to attack Yanping in order to receive a pincer attack. Yang Shuzhuang also hoped to resolve the war as soon as possible and specially summoned Liu Heding and Chen Jiliang on the 14th to discuss and decided to appoint Liu Heding as the Commander of the Eastern Route of the Minbei Bandit Suppression, leading the Liu Shangzhi and Chen Wantai brigades to attack the front of Yanping. The Gui Zhenyuan brigade will remain in Fuzhou. Fang Shengtong will be the Commander of the Western Route of the Minbei Bandit Suppression, leading the Chen Guohui, Xiao Shuxuan, Wang Zuqing, and Long Linqing divisions to attack the front of Youxi, and Lin Shuguo, Commander of the 2nd Marine Brigade, will lead the Lin Bingzhou regiment and the 2nd Provincial Police Brigade led by Liu Zongyi to advance from Pingnan and coordinate the attack on the flank of Yanping. Qian Yuguang, together with the Chen Huisheng and Huang Qilan guerrilla divisions, will advance from Gutian and coordinate the attack on the flank of Youxi. The mobilization order was issued on the 15th. Currently, the Lin Bingzhou regiment has departed from Fuzhou to Funing, and Lin Shuguo has also gone from Xinghua to Funing to command. The Liu and Chen divisions set off from the northwest gates on the 15th one after another. The general attack can probably begin in three to five days. However, the troops of the Lu division stationed below Shuikou were greatly affected by Qian Yuguang's defection and hastily withdrew the troops stationed at Gan, Zhe, Zhuqi, Dahu, and Guanyuan to Shuikou. At the same time, Datian was regarded as the gateway to Youxi. If Datian is lost, it will be difficult for Youxi to hold out for long. Two regiments of Youxi troops were urgently deployed to Datian to prepare to resist. Therefore, in the third phase of the war, the eastern route will center on Shuikou, and the western route will center on Datian. If these two places can be captured, Yanping and Youxi can be obtained with ease. (September 17)

Guangdong Province Sends Troops to North River to Suppress Bandits

Bandits in the Xiaobei River Harass Lianyang and its Vicinity

Zhang Zhen, Representative, Discusses Tranquility on the Guangdong-Fujian Border

Guangzhou Correspondence: Banditry has been rampant in the North River area of Guangdong Province recently. The most serious is in the Shaoguan and Yingde areas, where bandits in groups of hundreds loot and harass various villages. Huang, a local bandit leader in the Xiaobei River, openly raised the banner of a brigade commander and appointed Deng and Cai as regiment commanders to lead troops to harass various counties in the Xiaobei River. Local merchants have repeatedly telegraphed the province to appeal for help. In addition, according to returning guests from Nanxiong, the border between Guangdong and Jiangxi has been uneasy recently. A week ago, Nan'an, which is adjacent to Nanxiong, was attacked by hundreds of communist bandits. Residents evacuated to Nanxiong. This group of communist bandits was from Peng Cilong's department. After arriving in Nan'an, they extorted money from merchants and then fled south. Therefore, Nanxiong also raised its guard. The county police team and militia were sent to the border to guard against the communist bandits. Finding no opportunity, they turned and fled to Xinfeng. The authorities attached great importance to the report and have been increasing troops northward in recent days to suppress them as the opportunity arises. The method to be adopted is to first eliminate the bandits in the Xiaobei River to secure the border. In addition to immediately deploying the 2nd Battalion of the 3rd Independent Regiment stationed in Yingde to join the security team of the Public Security Bureau to search and suppress the Lianjiangkou area, fearing that the force would be too weak, the 1st Battalion of Wu Jianxiong's regiment and Li Yirong's division were also dispatched, along with a platoon of machine guns, on the morning of the 11th to Yingde on the Yuehan train to the Xiaobei River. It is also reported that Deng Hui's entire regiment of the 3rd Independent Regiment has recently been ordered to open north. The 1st and 3rd Battalions of Deng's division have been concentrated in the Beijiao parade ground and will take the Yuehan train to Maba, Wushi, etc. in one or two days to await orders. At the same time, the Eighth Route Army of Guangxi Province, in order to take into account the protection of the Fu River and the defense of northern Guangdong, has drawn part of the 59th Division to respond as the opportunity arises, and has also transferred Zhang Ruigui's division of the 1st Independent Brigade to join Deng Hui's division of the 3rd Independent Regiment to northern Guangdong to consolidate the security of Shao and Ying. As for the border defense of the East River, there have been rumors that the remnants of Lu Xingbang's department may flee to the Guangdong border. According to Kang Zichang, representative of Zhang Zhen stationed in Guangdong, the Guangdong-Fujian border is currently quite peaceful. The rumors of Lu's department harassing are just bandits posing as Lu's department. Xiang Hanping's division is conducting successive suppressions on the East River of Guangdong, and Fang Shengtong is coordinating with Liu Heding's division to go to northern Fujian to trấn慑 the Guangdong-Fujian border bandits. It will not be difficult to eliminate them in the near future. (September 13)

Cantonese People Oppose the Sha Mian Pass Permit

Embroidery Guild Asks the Municipal Government to Negotiate

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the great strike of Chinese people against foreigners in Sha Mian Concession in Guangzhou a few years ago, the discrimination against Chinese people has been less than in the past. Chinese people entering and leaving the concession are also said to be free. Unexpectedly, the French Concession in Sha Mian has recently established harsh regulations restricting the entry and exit of Chinese people. Chinese people carrying goods or livestock through the French Concession must pay a toll of one yuan. The most affected are the Chinese merchants who trade with foreign countries, because frequent entry and exit makes it difficult to pay the toll. This measure not only deals a great blow to merchants, but also damages our national prestige. The Embroidery Guild, which has always traded with foreign countries, specially reported the harsh regulations of the French Concession to the Guangzhou Municipal Government and requested that a protest be lodged. The original report roughly stated: "Our guild's business of embroidered scarves has always traded with foreign merchants. All goods must be delivered to Sha Mian. Since August 1 of this year, the French Concession Engineering Bureau has suddenly set up harsh regulations. Chinese people carrying goods and livestock, regardless of where they are carried to and the route they take, must pay a fee of one yuan and obtain a pass before being allowed to pass. The pass must be renewed every month, otherwise, regardless of the size of the item, it will be detained. It is now found that the bureau has issued more than 300 of these passes. Dozens of our guild's shops have had their goods detained because they did not know about this harsh regulation. Thinking that it is normal for merchants to trade goods back and forth, unless they pass through customs and places that must be inspected, there should be no delays or hindrances. Now the bureau prohibits the carrying of goods and even extends to livestock, which is truly rare and unreasonable. This behavior is nothing more than for the purpose of collecting fees, which can be concluded. Even if merchants pay the fee and obtain a pass, there are those who forget to bring the pass when delivering goods, or several partners deliver goods at different times. One pass is not enough to be distributed to several partners. There are various obstacles. However, this is only the difficulty in procedures. If we talk about national prestige, this pass is specially set up for Chinese people carrying goods and livestock, but not for foreigners. All goods entering the warehouses of foreign firms are not questioned before they are sold to Chinese merchants or after they have left Chinese merchants. What could be more unfair than this? Although Sha Mian is a joint British-French concession, it still belongs to Chinese territory. It is acting willfully and recklessly. If we do not argue based on reason, we are deeply concerned that the French Concession will set a precedent, and the British Concession will follow suit. Various special harsh regulations will follow one after another in all leased territories in the country. Thinking about the future, we secretly harbor hidden worries. If we demand improvement for the foreign abuse of Chinese workers, which is an obstacle to international equality, and now the French Concession in Sha Mian has newly established this harsh regulation, if we are willing to accept oppression, then national prestige is at stake, and business is hindered. Merchants have no choice but to endure momentary pain and make great sacrifices, refusing to obtain passes and unanimously suspending business as a passive resistance. However, if this continues for a long time, there is no end in sight, and the losses will be unbearable. Therefore, we clearly state our situation and humbly ask you to quickly lodge a protest and engage in serious negotiations with the French Consul, demanding equal treatment and canceling this pass in order to preserve national prestige and maintain commerce." After receiving the report, the Third Section of the Municipal Government filed a written protest. According to news from the French Consulate, they plan to change the method and exempt the pass fee, but the pass must still be issued. The Chinese side believes that the pass is one of the harsh regulations. If it is not fundamentally abolished, it is closely related to national prestige and will continue to fight to the end. (September 13 evening)

Russian Bandits Attack Stations on the Harbin-Manzhouli Railway Again

Harbin Correspondence: The Russian bandits on the Harbin-Manzhouli Railway are elusive and unpredictable. Those who reside in Shudu Yalu adopt a cautious attitude and have not taken much action in the past month. However, the Black Army is responsible for eliminating bandits, and the 15th Brigade led by Su Bingwen is fully responsible for suppressing them in that area. The 51st Regiment of the brigade has been maneuvering around Yalu County, taking a large encirclement posture, but has not yet clashed with the bandits. The Zhu Guofu gang took the opportunity to disturb the area along the line due to the emptiness of the line. Small groups of Russian bandits often appear between small stations, killing and looting merchants and travelers, and leaving as soon as the soldiers arrive. Therefore, corpses are scattered along the western road. In order to protect the safety of the railway line, the Black authorities ordered the 2nd Cavalry Brigade led by Cheng Zhiyuan to set out on the 11th to suppress the area along the road to clear the source of bandits. The direction of Cheng's brigade's departure is above Hailar on the Harbin-Manzhouli Railway. The Russian bandits then turned to disturb the area below Boketu. Yesterday, the headquarters of the road protection army here received a report that bandit traces had appeared near Andada Station, 300 li away from Harbin. Therefore, the authorities felt that it was difficult to suppress these cunning Russian bandits. On the evening of the 12th, the Balimu Station on the western line was almost taken by the bandits. Because the military and police force at the station was quite small, it had been besieged by bandits once a month ago, but the bandits did not succeed. On that evening, two Russian bandits first entered the station disguised as shoppers to scout the news. They were captured by the military and police. After questioning, they learned that a large group of Russian bandits wanted to invade the station and rob the 4th passenger train from Manzhouli to Harbin. Based on this, the garrison immediately notified all stations to pay attention and asked for help from the Boketu, Zhalantun, and Xing'anling stations. Before the reinforcements arrived, the bandits learned that their accomplices had been captured and sent people to demand their release within half an hour. The military and police, fearing that they were outnumbered, retreated towards Boketu and were attacked by bandits outside the station. They fought fiercely for a long time, and more than a dozen soldiers died. Then, 400 reinforcements from the Kang regiment in Boketu arrived and used armored vehicles to repel the bandits. Later, the 8th Cavalry Regiment of Zhalantun also sent 100 cavalrymen to search outside the station, but did not find the bandits. The 4th train, upon hearing the report on the evening of the 12th, stopped at Yalu Station. Passengers were panicked and waited until dawn before departing from Ya Station, delayed by half a day. It was not until 5:30 pm on the 13th that it arrived in Harbin. It was heard that the group of Russian bandits had not gone far, so the armored vehicle of the road protection army had not left the area to trấn懾 the bandits. (13th)

Suzhou

A Large Number of Refugees Disturb Qianzhuang: On the morning of yesterday (20th) at 10:00, more than 400 refugees from Hunan came from the Chefang area to Qianzhuang, demanding rice and grain from the village and surrounding the village to rob it. Shen Hongzu and two other families lost more than 800 yuan. Then they went to Tongli area and have now reported to the county government.

Competition in the Silk Industry: Suzhou is one of the silk producing areas in our country. Over the years, it has been occupied by imported goods, resulting in a great blow to business. The owners of silk businesses are deeply worried about this. Recently, there has been an advocacy for the use of domestic goods in various places, and people have changed their past habits. Therefore, the business of various silk shops has increased sharply and the doors are bustling with activity. Therefore, the same industry is also competing with each other, such as Guanqian Tongrenhe, Laorenhe, and Qiantai Xiang, etc., which are the most competitive.

Wuxi

Collision of Two Ships Leads to Conflict: The Xing Shun, a small ferry belonging to the local China Merchants Steam Navigation Bureau, set out from Qianzhou by tugboat at approximately 11:00 AM yesterday. Around noon, upon reaching the vicinity of Gao Bridge, it encountered a fully loaded open boat carrying Shaoxing wine coming downstream. Unable to avoid it, the ferry was struck violently by the wine boat. Liu Xingsheng, the captain of the ferry, seeing the damage to his vessel, began arguing vehemently with those aboard the wine boat. As a result, Liu Xingsheng was beaten and injured by the wine boat crew. Eventually, Dou Luyi, a local resident, intervened to mediate the dispute. He arranged for the owner of the wine boat to pay thirty yuan as compensation for the repair of the damaged ferry and Liu Xingsheng's medical expenses. Only then was the dispute resolved.

Theft Occurs in Xucheng Township: The Zheng Qin family, residents of Xucheng Township in Fuan, are reasonably well-off, but have no adult men in the household, only eight women. Their home comprises six courtyards. Last night, after midnight, after the family had gone to sleep, over ten bandits, speaking with Changzhou accents and armed with rapid-firing guns, electric torches, and knives, scaled the walls to enter the property, while others kept watch outside. After entering, they first tied up Zheng Qin and locked all the women in one room. Then, they ransacked boxes and chests, stealing whatever they could find. This went on for an hour before they departed with shouts. After they were gone, the family assessed their losses, finding that they had stolen over two hundred yuan in cash, over sixty articles of clothing, and gold and silver jewelry, amounting to a total loss of over eight hundred yuan. A detailed list of stolen items has been filed with the county government, requesting an investigation.

Injured Soldiers Prohibited from Extorting Additional Compensation: Reply to the Wuxi County Government and County Chamber of Commerce: Recently, individuals claiming to be representatives of injured soldiers have been frequently demanding compensation and causing disturbances at fish ponds in the western countryside. The county government telegraphed the provincial government's Department of Civil Affairs and the General Headquarters' Injured Soldiers Management Committee for instructions on whether local areas should provide additional compensation to injured soldiers stationed there. Yesterday, the Injured Soldiers Management Committee replied by telegram, stating that hospitals and injured soldiers throughout the region are prohibited from extorting fees from local areas, as had been promulgated by the General Headquarters. Regarding the issues raised in the inquiry, it stated that any injured soldiers causing disturbances should be dealt with severely according to the law, without leniency. The county government immediately forwarded the telegram to all relevant agencies for their information.

He dispatched the Xiaoxinqiao Defense Corps to investigate and apprehend him. On the 19th, the corps secretly went to Guotang Bridge, where they successfully captured Shen Borong and brought him to the district public office. On the 20th, District Chief Cheng prepared a document and sent the corps members to escort Shen Borong to the county government for interrogation.

Yangzhou

Chenjiagou Banditry: On the evening of the 18th, the Yang Guoqing cargo boat, sailing from Xinghua to Shaobo, departed Shaobo early on the 19th and headed towards Yangzhou, passing Chenjiagou near Xiaokouzi. Suddenly, they encountered a bandit boat, which fired a shot and ordered them to stop. Around 2:00 PM, the boat continued to Yangzhou, where the victim reported the incident to the authorities.

Changshu

Ransom Demands for Eight Abductees from Luhe Town: Regarding the abduction of eight people from Luhe Town, located at the border between this county and Taicang, it has been learned that the bandits cut off all traffic after arriving at the town. They first went to Cao Tiancheng's rice shop, abducting shop assistants Zou Bang'er and Cui Yiheng, as well as Cui Shouzhi, Cui Liangnan, Xu Songfen from Cui’s rice store, Wang, a woman, Zhou Jiaping, Tu Kuiyuan, and Yang Baoqing, shop assistants at Ma Wenrui’s store. They shot and killed Chen Xing, the owner of a tofu shop, on the spot. The bandits blindfolded all those abducted with black cloth, herded them to Baimaokou, and forced them into water up to their chests, soaking their clothes. Then, they took them by boat to Daan Port. Afterwards, relatives of the abducted hired a man named Jia from Hupu, providing him with three hundred yuan for expenses, to negotiate the ransom at the bandits' lair. However, the three hundred yuan was stolen, and the man returned in a wretched state. Recently, Yang Baoqing returned safely to the town, claiming that the bandits had ordered him to return home to deliver a message and announce the ransom amounts: fifty thousand yuan for Zou Bang'er, one hundred thousand yuan for the four members of the Cui family, and thirty thousand yuan for the three shop assistants from Ma Wenrui's store (including Yang himself). The exorbitant ransoms have caused widespread discussion. However, the bandits' lair at Daan Port has been dispersed by the army, and their current location is unknown. It is reported that the families of the abducted have gathered to discuss and send someone to the area again to search for the bandits' trail and negotiate.

Investigation Report on the Oil Well in Fenghuang District: Regarding the discovery of oil in the well at the home of Ya Yinglan in Tianzhuang Town, Fenghuang District, the county magistrate and District Chief Xu Jingyu have investigated and submitted a report. According to the report submitted by assistant Zhao Mengling and Qian Shuyu, who were dispatched by the district, they, along with Yang Dingyuan, the head of Tianzhuang Town, and Yachong, Ya Yinglan's son, were led to a small courtyard where they found an old well. They measured the depth to be just over one zhang, with the water level six chi and five cun from the bottom. When the water was drawn up, the surface was covered with oil slicks. They smelled it and confirmed it had the odor of petroleum. When they tried to ignite it, it would not burn or emit light. According to Ya Yinglan, the well suddenly changed on August 4th. For the first two weeks, the oil slicks were very thick and would ignite immediately when touched with a burning paper. After several heavy rains, the quality of the oil became slightly lighter. Recently, every day at 11:00 AM and 5:00 PM, there were surges of tide that mixed with the oil foam. The oil drawn up at these times was thicker and contained less water. The oil used to light the lamp was said to be the oil foam skimmed off the surface during the surges. Zhao Mengling and Qian Shuyu extracted well water and put it into two bottles to present for inspection. It is learned that District Chief Xu submitted the investigation report by Zhao Mengling and the two bottles of viscous water to the county government.

— Nantong

Measures to Quell Disturbances at the Border Between Tongzhou and Haimen: Major bandit gangs and salt smugglers are entrenched in the Daan, Niuhong, and other ports located at the border between Nantong and Haimen counties, causing disturbances. The provincial government has dispatched the Boxian and Junhe warships to join the provincial naval and land police to suppress them, and has ordered the governments of the two counties to promptly implement the following four measures: 1. Because the outer areas have sandbanks that prevent warships from entering and soldiers from wading ashore, a watchtower must be built between Daan and Niuhong ports, and cannons must be installed for defense. 2. Daan Port is the first district of Haimen, and Laohong Port is the tenth district of Nantong. Because of boundary issues, defenses have been neglected in the area where the two counties border each other. In the future, the two counties should complete the organization of the defense corps in these two districts within a time limit and jointly be responsible for defense. 3. First, eliminate the salt smugglers, and then assign the local defense corps and land and water police to strictly inspect travelers and strengthen defenses. 4. Local residents who know about bandit activities and fail to report them will be treated as accomplices to the bandits. The government must maintain strict confidentiality for those who report them.

The Dispute Over School Farmland to be Resolved by the Ministry of Education: The dispute between Tongzhou and Haimen counties over the reclamation and grazing of school farmland, which has been ongoing for two years, was recently submitted to the Ministry of Education for resolution. Minister Jiang ordered the Department of Education to instruct the two counties of Nantong and Haimen to have the Tonghai Reclamation and Grazing Company hold the rent from the school farmland in escrow until a decision is made in the case, and that neither party may forcibly collect it or cause trouble.

Ancient Cannon Unearthed at Chongzhong: While constructing the wall foundation at Chongjing Middle School in the northeast camp of the city, three ancient cannons were discovered. They were all made of iron and have been sent to the county for safekeeping.

Hospital Director Commits Suicide by Jumping into the Sea: Li Ruheng, a doctor and director of the Daishan Epidemic Prevention Hospital, boarded the Donghai ship, which was sailing from Wushantou to Ningbo on the 15th of this month, in the officer's cabin. Communist Bandits in Wen Prefecture Will Soon Be Eliminated: Wang Wenhan, the bandit suppression commander stationed in this port, had previously rushed to Wen Prefecture with his troops to suppress the bandits there. Shaoxing

Educational Surtax to Be Collected Regularly: The original county education fund in Shaoxing (derived from the collection of an autonomous surtax) was ordered by the province to be returned for autonomous use, with instructions to find other appropriate means of compensation. The Third County Education Conference decided to double the existing collection of school surtax to compensate for this. The Education Bureau submitted this proposal to the county, which in turn submitted it to the province for approval. An order was received to convene local public organizations to discuss appropriate measures. It was decided to pass the original proposal, with a one-year term. The provincial government has now approved this plan. In addition to the original collection of the school surtax, an additional half will be collected, amounting to four jiao per mu of field, two jiao per mu of land, and one jiao per mu of mountain land. County Magistrate Huang has set the date for the implementation of the additional surtax to begin on October 1st.

Local News

Tang Shaoyi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Unwilling to Comment on the Current Situation

Mr. Tang Shaoyi, accompanied by his wife and children, returned to Shanghai from Hong Kong aboard the Japanese ship Asama Maru. Shanghai Municipal Council Decides

To Increase Water Rates

Effective October 1st

The Shanghai Municipal Council held a board meeting the other day regarding the proposed increase in water rates. The council recognized that the increase was unavoidable and unanimously approved it. The decision has been officially passed and submitted to the Consular Body for filing. The company has decided to implement the plan on October 1st of this year. The company has responded to the opposition letters from various public bodies, including the Ratepayers' Association, the Municipal Ratepayers' Association, and the Citizens' Association.

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association received a reply from the Municipal Council yesterday, which stated: "To the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association, We acknowledge receipt of your letter of September 6th, forwarding the resolution of your representatives' meeting requesting a delay in the implementation of the water rate increase. Your letter has provided this council with an opportunity to explain the reasons for approving the rate increase. This council firmly believes that, after this explanation, your association will consider this council's measures to be appropriate, and the various misunderstandings in society will be dispelled. Article 10 of the contract signed on March 17, 1928, and published in the Gazette on April 6th of the same year stipulates that the price of water must be based on the net profit sufficient to pay the annual statutory dividend on all classes of stock. If the net profit in a given year is insufficient to cover the statutory dividend, the difference must be made up from the net profit of the following year. The dividend for the following year will be increased by the amount necessary to make up the deficit from the previous year, resulting in an increased rate. Article 13 stipulates that water rates should be revised every five years after July 1, 1929, but the effective period of the rates may be shortened at any time if both parties agree. According to this article, the current water rates were agreed upon to be effective for two years, from July 1, 1929, to June 30, 1931. The agreed exchange rate was two shillings and five and a half pence. The documents regarding the agreed rates were published in the Gazette on April 26, 1926. Due to the current sharp decline in the exchange rate, the water company's expenses are projected to be higher than in previous years. After calculating the income and expenses for the first four months of this year, the net profit for this year is far less than that of last year. In order to fulfill the obligations stipulated in Article 10 of the aforementioned contract, the company proposed an additional surcharge as a way to solve the problem. This council cannot sit idly by and allow the safety of a company responsible for supplying the public with essential goods to be jeopardized. If no remedial measures are taken, the company will be unable to pay the statutory dividend. The rate of this dividend was previously calculated to be sufficient to attract new capital to expand the company's projects to meet the ever-increasing needs of society. If your association believes that this council has overemphasized the interests of the shareholders in the aforementioned reasons, then when this council approved the plan, it considered that both the dividend losses for this year and the depletion of the average dividend reserve fund must be compensated for during the next rate period. If we do not seek remedial measures now, the water prices borne by users in the future will increase sharply. While this council is doing its best to plan remedial measures, it is also taking into account the economic stability of the company. Therefore, it has reached an agreement with the company to extend the current rate period until the end of next year, with a surcharge of two and a half percent. If the exchange rate rises to two shillings, the entire plan will be reconsidered. The two and a half percent surcharge has been estimated to be sufficient to cover this year's dividend. We are writing to inform you of this, and we hope that you will take note of it."

Shanghai Municipal Government

Strict Investigation of Resistance to the Forced Collection of Rent

The Shanghai Municipal Government was ordered to raise customs revenue bonds. The fundraising committee decided to collect two months' rent in exchange for bonds, as previously reported. It has been heard that some people are distributing leaflets inciting citizens to oppose this. The Municipal Government believes that the collection of rent has been agreed upon by the gentry and business leaders of this city and has been approved by Chairman Jiang. Moreover, the interest on the bonds is favorable, and the citizens will suffer no losses. The authorities believe that only reactionary elements would take the opportunity to disrupt the process, and they have secretly ordered the Public Security Bureau to conduct a thorough investigation.

Naval Cadets Studying in Japan to Set Sail

Commander of Japanese Fleet Hosted Them Yesterday

Mr. He Xikun, a naval cadet, and student Li Huiji, who were sent by the Ministry of the Navy to study in Japan, were led by Mr. Li Shijia, the Director of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of the Navy, to pay a visit to Vice Admiral Kōichi Shiozawa, the Commander of the First Overseas Training Squadron of the Japanese Navy, at 10:00 AM yesterday. They were greeted by military attache Kitaoka Haruo, who provided refreshments. During the meeting, Vice Admiral Shiozawa gave a speech, saying that this was the first time the Chinese Navy had sent cadets to study in Japan and that China and Japan were neighbors and large coastal countries in East Asia. He hoped that the cadets would contribute their superior knowledge and experience to their country after completing their studies, creating a powerful navy, which would not only be the honor of Japan but also the aspiration of China. Chen Shaokuan, the Vice Minister of Naval Affairs, is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai this morning (the 21st), and Vice Admiral Shiozawa will host a banquet at the Japanese Club on the evening of the 23rd to honor the cadets. The cadets are scheduled to depart on the Nagasaki Maru on the morning of the 23rd, accompanied by Li Shijia.

Recent News from the Kangzang Walking Corps

Since the announcement of the formation of the Kangzang Walking Corps, there has been an overwhelming response, and the original office space is no longer sufficient. The office has now been moved to No. 7, Lianzhi Lane, Baoshan Road, telephone number Zhabei 4446. Shipping News from the Upper Reaches of the Yangtze River

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Resumes Sailings on the Upper Reaches of the Yangtze River: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company originally had four ships sailing to Yichang and Shashi in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. However, due to the political situation in recent years, the sailings were suspended for nearly two years. Now that the Ministry of Transportation will stop military transportation and the requisitioned Yangtze River ships will be gradually returned to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The company, noting that foreign ships such as Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Nissin are competing to add direct Shanghai-Yichang ships and that there is a surge in the transportation of yarn and cloth, has decided that the Kuaili will resume direct Shanghai-Yichang service on the 23rd after arriving in Shanghai today. This is the first ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to resume direct sailings to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River in two years. In addition, the Jiangda has also been returned to Shanghai. Due to damage to the ship, it will be put out to bid for major repairs today. The Sanbei Company's Wuxing is also scheduled to come to Shanghai from upstream, after which it will be allowed to operate direct Shanghai-Yichang sailings to compete with British and Japanese ships for business on the upper reaches. The Wuhu will depart tomorrow. Taikoo's new ship, the Wuhu, has undergone major repairs for sixty days, completely remodeling the cabins with a beautiful layout. Its speed is even faster than originally planned, making it the fastest ship on the Yangtze River. It will move to the Taikoo Wharf in Puxi today to load cargo and passengers and is scheduled to clear customs on the evening of the 22nd. It will make stops along the way to Yichang, passing through Zhenjiang, Nanjing, Wuhu, Anqing, Jiujiang, Hankou, and Shashi, to benefit merchants and passengers. The crew and attendants will provide extra care to the cargo and passengers. The cabins are spacious and comfortable, the food is excellent, and the fares are inexpensive.

National Products Association

Preparing to Participate in the National Industrial and Commercial Conference

Soliciting Members' Opinions and Compiling Proposals

The China National Products Maintenance Association believes that the Industrial and Commercial Conference convened by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is of great importance to the development of the national products industry. It specifically telegraphed to request permission to send representatives to attend. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce replied by telegram that the person in charge of the association (Standing Committee Member Wang Jiean) had already been hired. The association has now notified all its industrial and commercial members to solicit opinions and compile proposals so that the Wang representative can submit them at the conference. The notification is transcribed below: Respectfully announced, we have recently received a telegram from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, which reads: "We have received your telegram. The Ministry has determined to convene an industrial and commercial conference to promote industrial and commercial policies, promote the development of production, promote overseas trade, and increase the national economy. We hope that the industrial and commercial sectors can express their opinions as much as possible to increase the effectiveness of the conference. Therefore, regarding the personnel attending the conference, Article 3, Paragraph 3 of the conference regulations stipulates that twenty to thirty people from domestic and overseas industries and businesses who are renowned should be hired. The people in charge of the association have already been hired. The opinions of national product manufacturers can be widely collected and proposals prepared, which will be submitted by the representatives of the association attending the conference for discussion. The Industrial and Commercial Department has stamped its seal for this reason. Having received this order, it was submitted to the 26th meeting of the 19th Executive Committee. In addition to the general plan prepared by the association, this telegram is sent to all manufacturers, asking them to send their heartfelt pain and hopes for improvement to the association within two weeks of receiving this letter. The association will compile the proposals, submit them to the representatives of the association attending the Industrial and Commercial Conference for discussion, and implement them. The Industrial and Commercial Department is waiting for instructions." The industrial and commercial sectors in China have suffered greatly in recent years and have reached a dead end. No one has appealed on their behalf. Fortunately, Minister of Industry and Commerce Kong has keenly seen the difficulties of the people and is deeply seeking to understand the hidden plight of businesses and has convened a national industrial and commercial conference. How can we not admire his great plan? The industrial and commercial colleagues of the national products sector should take advantage of this once-in-a-lifetime opportunity to express all the obstacles they have encountered, without exaggeration or concealment. They should send their opinions to the association on time so that the attending representatives can fulfill their duties. If they can strive for even a small amount of benefit at the conference, it will be an added assurance for the national products sector. Therefore, we send this notice in accordance with the regulations. We hope that your members will consider this to be a matter of life and death for our national products sector and will take advantage of this opportunity to submit their opinions as much as possible so that the government can adopt and implement them to benefit the people and secure the foundation of the country. We are eagerly awaiting your reply.

Wheat Flour Finally Approved for Customs Clearance and Northern Transportation

Two to Three Hundred Thousand Bags

The ban on transporting wheat flour from this port to the Tianjin port has been lifted for many days. However, the customs authorities only received a formal order yesterday. Therefore, the northern transportation of wheat flour was also delayed until yesterday before it was approved for customs clearance. Because there is still a lot of foreign flour in the north, Tianjin merchants are not very enthusiastic about ordering goods here. It is estimated that about 300,000 bags of wheat flour were declared yesterday. Furthermore, due to the lack of ships going north, many of those who declared customs clearance were still unable to ship their goods.

Various Silk Factories

Suspending Work Early Due to Lack of Raw Materials

Due to the lack of raw silk cocoons and the sluggish market and tight financial turnover, more than 40 silk reeling factories in Zhabei have suspended work early, one after another. It is estimated that more than 16,400 workers have been laid off. Most of the remaining silk factories will also suspend work early and resume operations after the spring cocoons are available next spring.

Informants Should Indicate Their Addresses

The Shanghai County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee has recently received many cases of reports from citizens in various districts requesting thorough investigation. However, these citizens did not indicate their addresses, which did not comply with the reporting procedures. The committee was also afraid that these people would make false accusations out of resentment, implicating innocent people. Therefore, it seemed difficult to deal with them rashly. It is now understood that the committee has formulated and will announce the reporting rules to the public. All informants should indicate their addresses to comply with the procedures and show their sincerity. Otherwise, the case will not be accepted.

Embroidery Industry Association

Meeting to Help Member Shi Xinchang

The Shanghai Embroidery Industry Association held an executive committee meeting at 8:00 PM the day before yesterday, with more than ten committee members present. Chairman Yang Yongrun first reported the purpose of the meeting, saying that the meeting was being held to request assistance for Shi Xinchang's house being forced to relocate by the landlord Xu Benji. Next, members Shi Xinchang and He Yunzhang stated that their company moved into the premises in the 13th year of the Republic of China. The houses were dilapidated and uninhabitable. When the engineers of the Engineering Bureau passed by, they saw that the interior was decaying and did not allow repairs, so they issued a notice to revoke the construction. At that time, they asked Xu Benji to rebuild, but he did not agree. The company was in a dilemma and had no choice but to invest more than 50,000 yuan to build a Western-style building and pay a tip of 7,000 yuan. Now, after only seven years, they are suddenly forced to relocate, and the company will inevitably go bankrupt. They requested assistance. Next, Zheng Baoyuan explained the assistance methods (omitted). After discussion, it was decided to: 1. Submit a petition to the Party Department to advocate for justice; 2. Send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, hoping that it would consider them as fellow members and resolve the matter; 3. Submit a petition to the Municipal Government's Social Bureau for a fair ruling; 4. Send a letter to the court for a fair judgment; 5. Declare the facts and reasons to various groups for assistance; 6. Send representatives to petition various parties; 7. Organize discussion groups based on the law and other proposals. The meeting then adjourned.

Overseas Chinese Federation

Asks for Relief for Disaster-Stricken Overseas Chinese in Pontianak

Approved by the Executive Yuan after being submitted by the Ministry of Interior

The Overseas Chinese Federation of the Republic of China telegraphed the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee, the Executive Yuan of the National Government, the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and the Relief Committee to provide relief to the overseas Chinese in Pontianak, Dutch Borneo, who were affected by the fire. It has been heard that the Ministry of Interior replied in a telegram: "The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Federation is aware that the overseas Chinese in Pontianak have suffered heavy losses in the fire, which is deeply concerning. It has been submitted to the Executive Yuan's meeting for deliberation and approval to allocate funds for relief." The Qiaoyin Relief Committee of the Ministry of Interior replied in a telegram: "The Overseas Chinese Federation is aware that the Huaqiao residential area in Pontianak, Borneo, Southeast Asia, has suffered a terrible fire and suffered huge losses. It is earnestly requested that you preside over the relief effort to show the central government's concern for the disaster-stricken overseas Chinese. Your association's concern for overseas Chinese is greatly appreciated. However, the funds for relief from our committee have already been allocated and there are no funds left. We will wait for a way to raise funds before reviewing and processing the matter." The Executive Yuan then took a further step to allocate relief funds and also resolved to submit a petition to the National Government to instruct the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to send resident consuls to investigate the disaster and offer condolences to the victims.

Salary Increase for Seamen Has Been Implemented

Seamen serving on various ships have not received a salary increase for several years. They have jointly submitted a petition to the Seamen's Shanghai Branch through various ship workers, guilds, dormitories, and clubs, which was forwarded to the Chinese Seamen's Industrial Federation. The federation sent members to consult with the Shipping Association, and a salary increase agreement was signed last month. However, although the agreement has been signed, the shipping companies have not yet fulfilled it. The Seamen's Federation has sent a letter to the Shipping Association inquiring about the matter. The Shipping Association has now replied with two letters, saying that the agreement has been implemented in full. The two letters are copied below: (1) Received a letter stating that the salary increase for seamen will be implemented from August 1st in accordance with the agreement. However, according to the workers of each ship, the companies have not paid the increased salaries. The association is requested to notify the shipping companies to issue the increased salaries to the seamen to prevent problems. After checking with the association, it was found that the agreement had been printed and distributed to all members for compliance. A letter from the Shanghai branch of your federation was received on the same matter, and another letter was sent to all members to comply with the agreement. A reply is hereby sent for your reference. (2) A letter was received stating that your association's letter No. 4492 requests that we urge the shipping companies to increase the salaries of seamen in accordance with the agreement. After checking the case, a letter from your association was previously received on the same matter, and another letter was sent to all members to comply with the agreement. Yesterday, we replied with letter No. 74. We received a letter from the Sanbei Shipping Company, stating that they had received letter No. 4486 and understood everything. The company had previously received a letter from the Shipping Association and had sent the letter to the captains of each ship for the information of each seaman. We are now sending a reply for your reference. As for the issue of salary increases for tallymen on each ship, it is being actively pursued.

Gongbuju Chinese Newspaper to Be Published

The Shanghai Times reported that the Shanghai Public Concession Gongbuju has been preparing to issue a Chinese-language newspaper. It is heard that the first issue will be published around the beginning of next month. At the Gongbuju board meeting the other day, the difficulty of publishing the English and Chinese versions of the newspaper at the same time was discussed. After reviewing the Chinese-language director's proposal letter and the sample newspaper, it was agreed that the Chinese directors did not object to publishing the Chinese version a few days later than the English version. Therefore, the Chinese-language director's proposal was approved, and the Chinese-language newspaper will be published on the Wednesday following the publication of each English version.

Total Statistics of Cholera Cases in the Past Three Weeks

The Shanghai Temporary Office for the Prevention of Cholera is very serious about checking for cholera bacteria. According to Dr. Wu Liande, the office sends people to five places every day: Shanghai Epidemic Hospital, Hongkou Epidemic Hospital, Red Cross Epidemic Hospital, Emergency Epidemic Hospital, and Public Shanghai Hospital, to check patients. If necessary, they will immediately go to the patient's home to check the population in their home. Once, four people with cholera bacteria were found in the home of a patient at the Hongkou Epidemic Hospital. Because the person had a strong antitoxin, the bacteria did not erupt and cause harm. They were injected with a preventive vaccine to kill the bacteria. It is also heard that the epidemic in Shanghai has weakened this year. From the beginning of summer to August 27th, no genuine cholera had been discovered. Genuine cholera began to be detected on August 28th. The following are the total statistics of cholera patients in the above-mentioned five hospitals in the three weeks from August 28th to September 18th: Shanghai Epidemic Hospital: 31 inpatients, 8 discharged, 5 deaths, and 19 currently hospitalized. Hongkou Epidemic Hospital: 16 inpatients, and 16 currently hospitalized. Red Cross Epidemic Hospital: 4 inpatients, 1 discharged, and 3 currently hospitalized. Emergency Epidemic Hospital: 4 inpatients, 2 discharged, and 2 currently hospitalized. Public Shanghai Hospital: 2 inpatients, and 2 currently hospitalized. In total, the five hospitals have 57 inpatients with genuine cholera, 5 discharged, 5 deaths, and 42 currently hospitalized.

Japanese Navy Returns Home After Term Expires

More than 70 soldiers of the Japanese Naval Landing Forces stationed in Shanghai have completed their service and were ordered to return to their country by Commander Minei yesterday. They returned to their country yesterday afternoon on the special service ship Muroto.

Basic Cooperative for National Goods Production and Sales to Hold Meeting

The Shanghai Basic Cooperative for National Goods Production and Sales, initiated by the Social Bureau, submitted its articles of association, which were revised by the Municipal Government. The revised articles stipulated that the cooperative would be composed of two types of members: Type A, family basic groups (referred to as Type A members), which include adult women of the Republic of China who have received elementary education and pledge to use domestic goods; and Type B, domestic goods production groups (referred to as Type B members), which include citizens of the Republic of China who manufacture or sell domestic goods. These articles were submitted to the Shanghai National Goods Factory Association and other groups for comments yesterday. A meeting will be held on the 23rd of this month to discuss and approve the articles, and then the organization will be started.

Reaffirming the Order Prohibiting the Use of Qing Dynasty Ceremonial Guards

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau issued a notice to all districts and teams yesterday, stating: "In order to comply with the order, a public letter was received from the Social Bureau, stating: 'According to a letter from citizen Zheng Jie, citizens in the city are still using Qing Dynasty ceremonial guards for wedding and funeral ceremonies, and the police are not interfering. A strict investigation and prohibition should be requested.' Previously, a joint announcement was issued to prohibit feudal-style wedding and funeral ceremonial guards, and your bureau was instructed to strictly prohibit them. Now, the situation is being reported, and a further letter is being sent to your bureau to investigate and instruct all districts to instruct all police officers to pay attention at all times and ensure that the prohibition is enforced in accordance with the law.' The order has been issued to investigate and prohibit this case, and the Social Bureau has jointly drafted provisional rules for prohibiting wedding and funeral ceremonial guards, which have been announced to the public. Why is the previous situation still occurring? The district is not implementing the order effectively, which can be seen. In addition to distributing the letter, we are now ordering the district chiefs to comply and instruct their subordinates to strictly prohibit the situation and not to be negligent. This is an urgent order."

Warning Women About Clothing

Public Security and Social Bureaus

Do Not Want Women to Be Barefoot

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau and the Social Bureau jointly issued a notice yesterday, stating: "Regarding the joint announcement, the people's clothing is closely related to social customs. The Ministry of Interior previously drafted clothing regulations and submitted them to the National Government for promulgation and implementation. The circulation of odd costumes and outfits has been prohibited. Recently, it has been discovered in the city that a small number of women are wearing gorgeous clothes without socks or wearing short socks and exposing their legs, flaunting through the city. This kind of bad habit originated with foreign women who flaunt their beauty as a way of demonstrating uniqueness. The ignorant women of our country are following suit, which is very detrimental to customs. In addition to ordering all districts to strictly prohibit such attire, this joint announcement is issued for the information of all women in the city. Do not intentionally violate the prohibition, or you will be punished." This is an urgent notice.

The Simma Road, Shiloo East branch of Weiya Restaurant is about to relocate to its newly constructed business building. The decor is splendid, with dozens of exquisitely spacious halls and rooms. Zhabei Small Fire

The Xie family residence, belonging to Xie Jinfa, a local resident, is located at Gongxing Bridge, Xibao Xing Road, Zhabei. Last night at around 11:00 PM, a fire broke out because a lot of rice straw was piled under the eaves, and a cigarette butt ignited it. The flames quickly spread and pierced through the roof, like a prairie fire. Upon receiving the news, the Zhabei Sections 1, 2, and 3 Fire Brigades immediately dispatched vehicles to put out the fire. It took some time to extinguish it. A total of three single-story houses were destroyed.

Recent Developments at the Second Work-Study Home for Vagrants

The former Songhu Reformatory on Song Park Road in Zhabei used to rely on donations. Since it was taken over by the Shanghai Charity Association in May of this year and renamed the Second Work-Study Home for Vagrants in Shanghai, regular and temporary expenses have been stipulated, and capable personnel have been selected to manage it. At the same time, the donation collection office was abolished, and fundraising was stopped, as had been announced in the newspaper. It has now been four months. The home previously had skills such as towel making, straw rope making, and paper making. Now, shoemaking, paper box making, and sewing have also been added. The products are of excellent quality and are quite popular in society. Even the apprentices are being reformed and learning skills, showing significant improvement compared to before. Recently, it has been reported that there are still bandits outside falsely using the names of the home and the Songhu Reformatory to forcibly solicit donations from businesses. The home has sent a letter to the police district requesting strict investigation and prosecution.
