Page 15

Local News 2

Yu Yahao Accuses of Marriage Fraud and Theft

Detectives Zhang Nai and Yang Xuejiu

Yang Xuejiu's sacrifice for love is open and honest

Zhang Nai traveled far to Japan but did not appear in court yesterday

Sharing Knowledge and Mutual Interests Zhang Nai, a technician at the Wuzhou Soap Factory, whose original name was Yu Xuelou, took the surname Zhang because he was also the heir to his maternal grandfather's family. In the autumn of 1923, when Zhang was studying at Beijing Normal University, there was a Wuxi girl named Yu Yahao who initially studied in the Chemistry Department of Beijing Women's Higher Normal School. In September of that year, she graduated and entered Beijing Normal University to continue studying chemistry. She became a classmate with Zhang, and because they shared knowledge and felt mutual interests, their relationship gradually deepened. Zhang repeatedly proposed to Yu, but was rejected each time.

Married in Wuxi after returning from the United States After Yu graduated and obtained a bachelor's degree, she returned south. Zhang also went to the United States to study. Since then, they were separated by vast oceans. However, Zhang still did not forget Yu and repeatedly wrote to Yu from the United States, vowing to never change his mind. Yu still did not easily agree. In 1927, Zhang returned to China from the United States and specially asked a matchmaker to speak to Yu's parents. Zhang also promised that he would never take a concubine. Yu finally agreed under the sympathy of her parents. On July 22, 1928, she officially married Zhang at the Wuxi Hotel.

Cohabiting in Xuhui and Advancing Household Expenses Not long after, they came to Shanghai and lived in No. 19 Zhiqingfang, Xujiahui. At that time, Yu was a teacher at the middle school department of Jinan University and Nanyang Model Primary School. Zhang was a technician at the Wuzhou Soap Factory. Zhang did not provide any household expenses and asked Yu to advance them temporarily. Yu's income and private savings spent on household expenses amounted to more than 2,236 yuan.

Transferring Affection to Ms. Yang Xuejiu Unexpectedly, Zhang suddenly became tired of this virtuous helper and fell in love with Ms. Yang Xuejiu, a famous painter and principal of Chengdong Women's School in Zhuhang Lane, Nanshi Huayi Street. All of Zhang's technician salary was spent on Yang. Yang knew that Zhang was already married, but did not care at all. Zhang transferred his love to Yang and regarded his wife as insignificant. Therefore, when Yu gave birth in January of last year, he did not return home day or night. Occasionally, when he returned home, he would find fault for no reason, or want to kill the baby, or threaten Yu to commit suicide with a knife, or deliberately push Yu to injure her, or even try to poison his wife with mold. He also wrote a suicide note to intimidate Yu. All kinds of actions were extremely bizarre.

Yu Yahao returned to Wuxi for recuperation Yu had no choice but to write to Yang Xuejiu's mother, Ms. Yang, asking her to advise her daughter not to destroy other people's families, but it was to no avail. On February 12 of this year, Yu accompanied her sick son to Guangren Hospital for hospitalization. On March 11, her son died young. Zhang did not show any grief or concern. At this time, Yu was still pregnant. Her mother saw that her beloved daughter was deeply saddened and became more miserable in Shanghai. Therefore, she called Yu Yahao back to Wuxi for recuperation.

Zhang and Yang were married at Moore Memorial Church The Shanghai residence was only left with servants to guard it. Unexpectedly, after Zhang's wife returned to Ningbo, he dismissed the servants, returned the house, and ordered his birth mother, Yu Zhang, and his sister, Gong Yu, to secretly move all of Yu's clothes and other items to No. 53 Nanmeiyuanli, Gonghe Road, Zhabei. On May 24, Zhang Nai and Yang Xuejiu's parents publicly presided over the wedding at Moore Memorial Church on Samma Road, and Zhang and Yang became married from then on.

Prosecuted for Marriage Fraud and Theft After Yu Yahao recovered from her illness and returned to Shanghai, she negotiated with Zhang, but it did not have a satisfactory result. She then hired lawyer Li Zuyu to file a criminal self-prosecution with the Special District Local Court, accusing Zhang Nai, Yang Xuejiu, Zhang's mother, Yu Zhang, Zhang's sister, Gong Yu, and Yang's mother, Ms. Yang, of marriage fraud and theft, requesting that they be punished according to the law. In addition, she filed a private lawsuit requesting that Zhang Nai be ordered to repay the household expenses of 2,236 yuan, compensate for the taken clothes of 3,000 yuan, and pay for the plaintiff's living expenses and future upbringing expenses of 30,000 yuan.

Yang Xuejiu was arrested by the court The court has opened a court twice based on the allegations, but because the main defendants Zhang Nai and Yang Xuejiu were all at large, the trial could not proceed. The plaintiff was allowed to request the issuance of arrest warrants to bring them to court for further interrogation. It is now known that Zhang Nai has already fled to Japan and has not returned to China, so it is difficult to arrest him. Although Yang Xuejiu also traveled to Japan with Zhang at the same time, she has recently returned to Shanghai and still lives in Chengdong Women's School. At 3:00 PM the other day, the patrol room specially sent detectives to Nanshi to cooperate with the local police station to send additional detectives to the women's school to arrest Ms. Yang Xuejiu and bring her back to the Special District Court for temporary detention in the women's detention center.

She was brought to court for questioning yesterday morning The case was originally scheduled to be reopened next Tuesday afternoon. Yang's family feared that Ms. Xuejiu would not be able to endure the taste of iron windows for a few more days, so they hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to request bail. Therefore, Judge Cheng Shangfeng specially opened the fifth court yesterday morning to hear the bail issue. The plaintiff, Yu Yahao, arrived in court with her mother, wearing a yuan-colored silk cheongsam. The defendant, Yang Xuejiu, was wearing a western suit with a beige coat with a silk flower on her chest, standing in the defendant's box, calm and composed.

The judge said that he would first interrogate the facts. Advocate Cheng first asked about her name, age, and address. Yang said that she was 28 years old, a native of Shanghai, living in Chengdong Women's School, and currently unemployed. Lawyer Jiang immediately requested that the case be adjourned because he had just been entrusted with the case and all the defense procedures needed to be investigated before he could start. Judge Cheng said that he would first interrogate the facts today.

She went to Japan with her after the wedding Judge Cheng then asked Yang what kind of person Zhang Nai was and whether he had other names. Yang replied that she did not know who Zhang Nai was. Her husband's name was Yu Xuelou. She continued to ask about the wedding process. Yang replied that she was married at Moore Memorial Church on May 24. She was completely in charge of the wedding. She had a mother and three younger sisters and one older sister. Because her mother did not approve of her free marriage, she never discussed it with her mother until the night before the wedding. Her mother did not attend the wedding. Of course, her mother did not preside over the wedding. She hired a pastor to be the wedding officiant. After the wedding, she moved to rooms 305 and 307 of the Dongya Hotel. Then she went to Japan with him. She went to Japan to sell paintings. She recently received a telegram from her mother and returned to Shanghai on the 18th. When she left, her husband had already gone to Kyoto. She left a letter to say goodbye. Her husband is also currently unemployed.

She only agreed to marry him after knowing that he was divorced Judge Cheng also asked if she knew that Zhang Nai was also the heir to his maternal grandfather's family. Yang replied that she knew about this and her husband had told her that he had divorced his ex-wife. But she did not ask who his ex-wife was, nor did she ask if there was any evidence when he divorced his ex-wife. She only married him because she knew that he was already divorced. Her husband used the surname Yu. She did not see the newspaper announcement, so she did not know what his intentions were. Her mother never told her that her husband had sent a letter to her. Although she had known him for seven or eight years, she still did not know about his family situation. Chen Shizhen, who introduced them to each other, was now dead.

First claiming to go to Hangzhou, then to Ningbo Judge Cheng turned to the plaintiff, Zhang Yu Yahao, who spoke with a northern accent and said that Ms. Yang's claim that she had divorced Zhang was not true. On the night of December 3 last year, Zhang suddenly said that he would go to Hangzhou the next day. When asked what he was going to do, he did not answer. She asked to go with him, but was refused. The next day, she sent him to the train station and saw that Zhang had bought a ticket to Nanjing. Later, she learned that Ms. Yang was also in Nanjing and was living with her husband in the Jiaotong Hotel Room 27. Yang's mother was also in Nanjing. The express letter she sent to her was mailed from Xujiahui. Now, all the items in her house have been taken away. It is difficult to find the receipt for this express letter. Please investigate the guest name book of the hotel, which will be able to prove the facts she described.

Yang said that she was also quite apologetic to Yu Lawyer Li then presented the two letters written by Yang Xuejiu to the court. Judge Cheng glanced at them and handed them to Yang for review and asked if they were written by her. Yang admitted that the letters were sent to a friend with the surname Hu, asking him to investigate the attitude of Wuxi towards this matter. She said that she did not know that Xuelou was Zhang Nai at first, and that she realized that the so-called divorce that he had previously mentioned was actually his first marriage, not the current plaintiff. Therefore, she asked Hu to investigate. After the investigation, she was quite apologetic to Ms. Yu.

Ms. Yang is willing to sacrifice for love Judge Cheng instructed Yang, since you know that Zhang Nai came to divorce from Wuxi, Zhang has actually deceived you. Why don't you file a lawsuit against him? Yang replied that although she knew she had been deceived at this time, her feelings had not yet been broken. And since she has already sacrificed for love, she could not bear to proceed with the prosecution and instead sought a way to mediate.

A great debate arose over the issue of bail Lawyer Jiang then defended the defendant, saying that the defendant did not intentionally resist the summons. After receiving the telegram, she rushed back from Japan and arrived in court. What she said today is all true. She was also deceived by Zhang Nai. Judging from her open and honest attitude, it can be determined that she is not likely to flee. She should be allowed to post bail and wait for the summons outside. Lawyer Li expressed opposition, saying that based on the defendant's letters, it can be known that the defendant knew that Zhang Nai had a wife when she married him. The plaintiff still has various evidence that will be presented at the next hearing to further prove that the defendant's claim that she only returned to Shanghai from Japan on the 18th is not credible. The plaintiff knows that the defendant has been in Shanghai for a long time. All of this can be investigated. Therefore, at a minimum, the defendant must post a shop guarantee.

Released on ordinary bail to be available upon summons Judge Cheng then ruled that the defendant, Yang Xuejiu, be released on ordinary bail to be available upon summons. The next hearing was rescheduled for 3:00 PM next Tuesday afternoon. Yang's relatives who were in court to listen to the hearing posted the ordinary bail bond in court yesterday afternoon and were temporarily released on bail.

Shanghai Danger

Flipping Opera Party Active

Xie Xunxia was deceived but did not publicize it

The captain of the Weihai ship is relatively shrewd

Paper money stacked up to tens of thousands

These moths should be severely punished

The world famous master player willing to bet one cent and determine the result Xie Xunxia (also known as Xie Xuan) from Pingyang, Zhejiang is skilled in the art of chess and has no equal. Xie has a bookstore in Shanghai and his family lives at 222 North Sichuan Road. Last month, two people suddenly came to his store saying they wanted to buy books. Xie and Kuan chatted and learned that they were from the same hometown. They were extremely welcoming to each other and after some pleasantries, they learned that the two guests were named Li Xianting and Pan Guozhong who lived in room 65 of the New New Hotel. Since then, they have been in contact with each other. On the 17th of last month, Li and Pan visited Xie again and said that a Japanese was also good at chess and admired Jun's name and wanted to bet one cent to determine the result. Xie happily displayed his skills because he found a true friend. They agreed to meet at 10 a.m. the next day in room 65 of New New.

There was no chess set and no intention of playing chess When they arrived on time, they glimpsed the name of the resident of New New on the guest plate of room 65 which had changed to the surname Wang. They intended to approach the room and ask about the reason for the change of surname. When they reached the door of room 65, they saw Pan waiting outside the door. They were invited to enter and besides Li and Pan, there were two other guests. After Li introduced them, they learned that one was Taiwanese Cai Tingbang and the other only knew his surname was Liu. Looking around, there was no chess set and everyone showed no intention of playing chess, so they asked Li about it.

A pistol was suddenly drawn demanding 5,000 yuan At this moment, Liu suddenly closed the door tightly and shouted at Xie, "Your business is going very smoothly and we are extremely impoverished. We have spent a lot of energy and effort to detect your preferences, so we have specially invited you to come here with words. We don't want to play chess, we want to borrow 5,000 yuan. You have already been caught. If you don't agree, I'm afraid it will be difficult for you to return." Xie was fearless after hearing this and told him that he was not a rich merchant, how could he have thousands of gold. If you don't believe me, you can dispose of me. Seeing Xie's strong attitude, Liu took out a pistol and threatened him in every possible way. The two sides faced each other for a long time and Xie agreed to give 1,000 yuan.

They got 750 yuan with a voucher only because they did not carry the money with them, so they wrote an IOU. Those people then sent their party to Xie's house to collect it. After a while, the person who took the money returned and said that they only got 750 yuan. Those people then kidnapped Xie and went to Ma Huo Road before letting him go. Before leaving, they told Xie not to report to the police, otherwise there would be more severe measures to deal with him, so Xie kept the secret as if it were a deep ear. It has been a long time and he only occasionally revealed it to his relatives and friends, but those people have not been seen. It is believed that they have fled, but in fact, Li and others are still in the concession practicing their intimidation career.

The captain of the Weihai ship came to Shanghai because of this It has now been detected that Wu Jian, the captain of the Weihai ship of the Northeast Fleet and a native of Pingyang, came to Shanghai for official business at the beginning of this month and stayed in room 1 of the Nanjing Hotel on Edward Road. At 10 a.m. the other day, Li Xianting, also known as Wang Liyu, and Huang Lushen from Fujian went to visit Wu. At that time, because they were from the same hometown, he agreed to see them even though they had never met before. Li then said that his master had assets of tens of millions and many concubines. Now, the third concubine had taken a huge amount of money and taken the master's son to Yantai. Because he knew that the teacher had been stationed there for the longest time, he came to ask him to pay attention to it. Wu immediately agreed.

They agreed to go and see the runaway concubine's photos Li also said that the photos of the runaway concubine were still in room 417 of the Oriental Hotel where he lived and asked him to come along and view them so that he would not be confused when they met in the future. At this time, Wu felt that Li was too casual and was pestering someone he didn't know. He was very suspicious. He suddenly recalled what his friend Li Chuqun had said about Xie Xunxia being deceived. He carefully examined Li's face and it was very similar to the face of the deceiver mentioned by Li's friend. He did not reveal his expression and agreed to visit the East in the afternoon to return the visit. Li and Huang happily left.

Report to the detectives and arrest three people Wu then asked someone to invite Xie to his residence to inquire about the details of the deception. He expected that Wang Liyu was Li Xianting. He reported it to the Old Gate Patrol Room and dispatched detectives Liang Chengyu and Wang Shusen to rush to the East to arrest Li Pan Huang

Page 16

the three people and Zhu Lian together.

Continued Capture of Li Song and a Taiwanese Man

During the search of the room, the suitcase was found to contain banknotes from the Bank of the Underworld, totaling 25,000 yuan. Subsequently, Li’s adoptive father, Li Song, and a Taiwanese man, Cai Tingbang, were apprehended and brought back to the police station. The police chief interrogated them. According to Li's statement, his real name is Wang Xianting, while Zhu Lian stated that he was a staff officer in the Zhenjiang Fortress Command. He had taken leave to visit his friend at the Youhua Hotel in Shanghai. Wang Xianting visited Zhu at the Youhua Hotel a few days ago. Hearing of this, Li came out to meet them. Although they did not know each other, they were fellow villagers, so they started talking. Wang then invited him to his residence for a chat to relieve boredom, which led to his arrest.

The Taiwanese man was handed over to the Japanese consulate. Xie also went to the police station to declare that Zhu Lian was definitely not present when he was swindled. The police chief released Zhu. Cai Tingbang, being of Taiwanese籍, was instructed to be escorted to the Japanese领事馆 for interrogation. The remaining four people were escorted to the Special District Court yesterday morning, where Judge Xu presided over the interrogation. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated that Wang Xianting and others were being prosecuted under Article 370 of the Criminal Law, requesting strict punishment.

Bank of the Underworld Notes Used as Chips According to Wang Xianting's statement, he told Xie at the time that there was a Japanese man who was good at Go, referring to Cai Tingbang. Later, Cai was unwilling to play Go, so they switched to gambling on "One Two Three Four." Xie lost 1,250 yuan and, after repaying 750 yuan, still owed 500 yuan. Bank of the Underworld notes were used as chips during the gambling. Judge Xu then questioned the other defendants one by one and ordered them to be remanded in custody for another seven days for further questioning.

Blackmail of Shanghai College President Liu Zhanen

The Bandit Zhou Amao Apprehended

Liu Zhanen, Exhausted, Reports to the Police Station

Many Detectives Disguised, Ambushing from All Sides

Negotiation on the Third Floor of the Central Hotel

Beer Bottle as Signal, Plan Not Secret

Liu Zhanen, President of Shanghai College in Yangshupu, received a blackmail letter from bandits a month ago demanding a large sum of money. Liu ignored it. A few days ago, another letter arrived with very strong language, stating that if he continued to ignore it, they would resort to final and appropriate means. They also arranged a meeting place on the third floor of the Central Hotel on Zhengfeng Street, Hubei Road, with a beer bottle as a signal. Liu, under the pressure of the bandits' forces, had no choice but to report the situation to the General Inspectorate of the Central Police Station and request an investigation. Liu Shaokui, Chief of the General Inspectorate of the Central Police Station, upon hearing the news, secretly dispatched detectives disguised as ordinary people and personally led Chinese and foreign detectives to wait on the third floor of the Central Hotel yesterday afternoon. After a while, someone came to meet him, and he was immediately arrested. As the jurisdiction of the hotel belongs to the Old Gate Police Station, the blackmailing bandit, Zhou Amao from Ningbo, was temporarily detained at the police station and scheduled to be transferred to the court for investigation tomorrow.

Will Be Built in the Public Concession

Architect Gang Da Drawing Up Plans

The "Great American Evening News" reports that a twenty-one-story building will be constructed between Jing'an Temple Road, Park Road, and Baker Road to house a hotel and theater. Construction is scheduled to begin in early spring next year, with an estimated cost of 2.5 million taels, funded by a real estate company. It is reported that all procedures for the renovation have been arranged, and the construction license from the Public Works Department of the工部局 has also been obtained. The company's board of directors is currently reviewing the final drawings, and tenders for the purchase of materials are expected to be invited in early November, with the contractor to be determined. The architect drawing up the plans for the building is Gang Da, and everything is extremely novel and beautiful. Once completed, it will likely be the most magnificent and tallest building in the Far East.

Public Works Bureau Seeks Navigation Personnel

Graduates of Merchant Marine Schools

Starting Salary of 120 Yuan

The Municipal Public Works Bureau is planning to expand the city's ferry service with longer routes and add cross-river ferries. The third and fourth long-distance ferries have already been launched on September 8 and are expected to be completed and operational by the end of November. The three cross-river ferries are being built by the He Machinery Manufacturing Factory and have also begun construction. Recognizing the need to find navigation personnel for the new ferries in advance, the Bureau has specified the following recruitment methods: 1. Qualifications: Citizens of the country, aged 25 to 35, who have graduated from a merchant marine school in China or abroad, have proven navigation experience, possess some mechanical knowledge, are physically fit, have no bad habits, and are able to endure hardship. 2. Salary: Monthly salary ranges from 120 to 180 yuan in national currency. Those who wish to apply may submit their resume, along with supporting documents and a 4-inch half-length photo, to the Bureau (Fourth Section, Municipal Government Road, Fenglin Bridge, Shanghai) before October 10 of this year. Suitable candidates will be contacted for an interview, and the original documents will be returned to those who are not selected.

Shipping Magnate Da Lai Coming to Shanghai as Scheduled

October 3rd

Robert Dollar, the American shipping magnate, has seventeen giant ships on the Pacific route. In recent years, competition with British and Japanese shipping merchants in Sino-American shipping has been fierce, especially this year. This year, imports and exports on this route are even more lacking. Dollar has also invested 30 million US dollars to build two large mail ships, 625 feet long and with a displacement of 35,000 tons, with a speed of 21 nautical miles per hour. The ships are also equipped with airplanes, opening a new era in Far East shipping. Recently, one of the two new ships will be completed by the end of this year. Dollar, in order to expand Pacific shipping, is personally visiting major ports around the world. He arrived in Shanghai from San Francisco yesterday on his company's Madison轮. According to a telegram, he is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on October 3rd. Shi Ting, a senior executive of the Shanghai office, has already gone to Japan to welcome him and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on October 3rd. American businessmen in Shanghai will hold a meeting to welcome him after his arrival.

Current Status of Grain Transportation

Hunan Rice: Almost No Hunan Rice Transported to Shanghai (Hunan Rice Eased Restrictions) A small portion was first loaded starting on August 22. It was reported that the original plan was to load one million shi to Shanghai and two million shi to Nanhua ports by the end of this year. However, because the Hunan government had to extract an exit passport tax of five yuan per bag, the grain merchants in various places believed that the cost was too high due to the heavy tax, so they all stopped collecting and transporting. They unanimously demanded a reduction in the exit passport tax, but the Hunan government, due to budget concerns, has not agreed to reduce it, resulting in the suspension of Hunan rice exports. Recently, there has been no Hunan rice loaded on the upper Yangtze River ships for transshipment to Shanghai.

Jiangxi and Anhui Continue to Have Rice Arriving: After Jiangxi rice was allowed to be exported on September 1, several batches have been continuously transported to Shanghai from Jiujiang, totaling 20,000 to 30,000 bags. Yesterday, two more batches, totaling more than 6,800 bags, arrived on British and Japanese Yangtze River ships and have been unloaded at the Hongkou warehouse. Anhui Rice: Recently, with the new rice coming onto the market in Wuhu, southern Anhui, 600 bags of Anhui rice have been transported to Shanghai for the first time. (Note: Anhui rice has not been transported here for a long time, so this is the first batch to arrive in Shanghai.)

County Public Security Bureau

Apprehends Taixing Bandit Gang

The Shanghai County Government received a document from the Taixing County Government政务 police a few days ago, stating that bandit gangs have been rampant in the county, disrupting the local area, and that all firearms were purchased and transported from Shanghai. Knowing that many bandits were hiding in Shanghai, they brought along informants to Shanghai to apprehend them and requested assistance. County Chief Yan immediately ordered Director Shen of the Public Security Bureau to personally lead Captain Qi of the Detective Team and others to first capture Lu Zhang'er at the Shanghai-Taicang Railway Station. They immediately took him to the bureau for interrogation. According to his confession, the bandit gang's headquarters was located in Liuhe. Therefore, Director Shen led the entire detective team, all armed, in automobiles to Liuhe that night. Unexpectedly, the bandit gang had already heard the news, so there was no one in the headquarters. Later, they saw a young bandit, Zhang Hongjing, thirteen or fourteen years old, wandering around there, so they detained him. After questioning him, they learned that the bandit gang was hiding in the town's inns. They went to the inns and captured four bandits. They escorted all the captured bandits back to Shanghai to the bureau overnight for interrogation. They confessed that there were still accomplices hiding in Tangqiao, Pudong. Yesterday morning, they sent detectives to arrest one more bandit and ordered them to be detained together pending instructions. The names of the seven bandits captured are: 1. Lu Zhang'er, 2. Zhang Hongren, 3. Wang Koushan, 4. Wang Tianfu, 5. Liu Zixiang, 6. Xu Mingzhou, 7. Zhou Shougen. The Pengpu Township Defense Corps also captured seven people, including Diao Yutang, a few days ago, and they have now been transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Therefore, the County Public Security Bureau ordered detectives to go and pick them up yesterday afternoon so that they could be escorted to Taixing for trial. However, the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau stated that they had not been pre-trialed and did not understand the situation, so they were ordered to be temporarily detained. It was later learned that the County Public Security Bureau is scheduled to send detectives to escort the captured bandits to the Taixing County Government for trial today, Sunday.

Zhu still failed to appear during the continued trial yesterday morning, while Chiang Wan-chen came to court with lawyer Ni Jiong. Chiang was still young and, without makeup, her face looked sallow. However, Chiang firmly claimed that the opium paraphernalia belonged to her grandmother, and lawyer Ni defended her, saying that Chiang Wan-chen's grandmother, Zhou Huang, was old and sick. Whenever she came to Shanghai, she stayed at Chiang's house, and when she fell ill, she had to smoke opium. The paraphernalia actually belonged to her. Wharf Thugs Demand Overnight Fees

Wang Ahua Arrested and Taken to Court

Recently, in the Pujiang area of ​​the South City, a group of vagrants have been found. Every time various cargo ships arrive at the port and have not yet unloaded, they spend the night in the Pujiang River waiting to be unloaded the next morning. They form gangs and extort money from the cargo ship owners, calling it "overnight fees," ranging from two or three yuan to an uncertain amount. Therefore, the shipowners are all suffering from it. The night before, a ship carrying raw salt materials from the Wu Gan Jingyan Company from another port was moored next to the Dachu Warehouse Wharf. In the evening, many hooligans from Shaoxing, including Wang Ahua (陈阿华), extorted the aforementioned overnight fee. The ship's crew, fearing their ferocity, dared not resist and secretly went to report the situation to the Water Patrol Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and requested an arrest. Detectives were dispatched and arrested Ahua. After taking him to the team, he was ordered to prepare a document to be sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Chen Jigen Dies from Gunshot Wound

Chen Jigen, who lived at No. 66, Xinmin Road, Tangshan Road, went out at 7 PM on the 9th of this month to his uncle's house along the river. On the way, he suddenly heard a gunshot behind him. Just as he was about to turn around, a bullet entered his back, and blood flowed like a torrent. Chen ran with the wound to his uncle's house and was sent by car to Tongren Hospital for treatment. After examination by the doctor, it was found that the gunshot wound was quite serious, and he died at 3 AM the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo of the Special District Court went to the scene to investigate. He took his seat and said that the Western police reported that the case seemed to be an assassination, with no other suspicions. However, it was doubtful that the deceased was able to run such a long distance after suffering such a serious gunshot wound. Mr. Guo then asked the sister of the deceased, Mao Chen, if the deceased had any enemies outside. She replied that she did not know. He then concluded that Chen Jigen was indeed shot and assassinated while alive. The police station was ordered to strictly apprehend the murderer and bring them to justice. The corpse was handed over to Mao Chen for coffin burial.

One Woman Married Twice

Gan Hongqing Extremely Frustrated

Gan Liangzhen Unable to Accept It

Gan Liangzhen from Nanjing has a son named Gan Hongqing, who is 28 years old this year. In 1926, Gan Liangzhen hired Xu Guisheng as a matchmaker in Shanghai to betroth the daughter of Wang Yaoting, a fellow villager living in Xieqiao, as his daughter-in-law. The woman is 21 years old this year. At that time, because the woman was only 16 years old and not yet of marriageable age, it was agreed to marry in three years. Unexpectedly, in 1927, Wang Yaoting received a better proposal from another family and remarried his daughter to another family. She has now given birth and become a mother. However, after the three-year agreement of Gan Liangzhen and his son expired, they came to Shanghai to welcome the bride, but Wang's family had already moved and their whereabouts were unknown. A great marriage was ruined. Gan Hongqing was frustrated and wanted to die, and left home. Nothing in his life could be more unsatisfactory than this. Gan Liangzhen, unable to marry a daughter-in-law and angered by the departure of his beloved son, felt unable to accept it. Therefore, he looked for the matchmaker Xu Guisheng to argue and investigate, but Xu was a matchmaker from the Qian family and had no major responsibility, so Gan could do nothing. However, Xu was also unwilling to interfere in other people's affairs. On the day before yesterday, he found out that Wang lived in Zhuangjia Road in Ximen and notified Gan Liangzhen to go to Wang's house to ask for marriage. Wang was shocked and honestly said that he was willing to pay a subsidy of 40 yuan to cancel the marriage agreement. However, Gan felt that the loss was too small and refused to agree to discuss it further. Fearing that Wang would escape, he ordered a guarantor to be found. Jin Changqi, a neighbor, acted as a guarantor and agreed to continue negotiations yesterday. Unexpectedly, Wang avoided the trouble and hid. Gan then twisted Jin and accused him at the First Section of the Second District and handed Wang Yaoting over to the District Court for trial.

One Person Drowns

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education

Retaining Chen Bulei, Director of the Zhejiang Education Department

Chen Bulei, Director of the Zhejiang Education Department, once again submitted a request to the Ministry of Education to resign. The Ministry of Education earnestly retained him and ordered him to do his best and not to entertain any thoughts of resignation.

Ministry of Education Investigates Secondary Education

In order to investigate the educational status of secondary schools in various provinces and cities for the purpose of statistical collation, the Ministry of Education has specially formulated an investigation form and issued a general order to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities. The "Certain Secondary School Investigation Statistical Form" and the "Certain City Education Department and Bureau Secondary School Investigation Statistical Form" are recorded below, along with the instructions for filling them out.

Explanation of the Statistical Form for Certain Secondary Schools in the Eighteenth Year

1. The form is 44 cm high and 30 cm wide.

2. This form is applicable to all types of secondary schools. Each school must fill it out itself and submit it to the ministry and bureau for forwarding. In addition to sending one part to the ministry, the ministry and bureau that it passes through must have a copy for compilation and statistical collation.

3. After filling in the name of the province, city, and county at the top of the form, fill in provincial, municipal, county, or private, and then fill in the school name. If there is no "middle school" in the name, the two words "middle school" in the table should be crossed out.

4. The method of filling in the grades and departments in the student column: one department occupies one space, and the name of the department and the total number of grades are recorded. For example, if a junior high school has three grades and a total of eleven classes, it should be filled in as "Junior High School Department, a total of eleven grades, so many boys, so many girls, so many in total" (the total number of eleven grades). The order of arrangement of each department: first junior high school, then senior high school general department, then senior high school normal department, then senior high school agricultural department, then senior high school industrial department, then senior high school commercial department, then household affairs department, then rural normal school or short-term normal training class, then vocational department.

5. The statistics of graduates start from 1918, because there were statistics from the former Beijing Education Department before 1918, but after that, they were missing. Although this form is a statistical table for 1929, this column may as well go back ten years. The files of each school are there for inspection, which is not difficult, and the ministry will communicate and integrate to facilitate verification. Each school that was established later and only has graduates after 1918 should fill in the graduates of the first year.

6. Full-time and part-time teachers and staff: A full-time teacher is one who teaches only at this school and does not hold any position inside or outside the school. Otherwise, they are a part-time teacher. A full-time staff member is one who holds a position only at this school and does not hold any position inside or outside the school. Otherwise, they are a part-time staff member. If the principal also teaches a subject, they should be listed in both the part-time teacher and part-time staff sections.

7. Teachers and staff with degrees from normal universities in the two columns of teachers and staff refer to those who graduated from a normal university and obtained a bachelor's degree. Those who graduated from the higher normal school department of the normal university should be classified as graduates of a higher normal school.

8. University graduates refer to those who graduated from a university undergraduate program and obtained a bachelor's degree. Those who graduated from a specialty within the university are classified as graduates of a technical school. Preparatory graduates are classified as other.

9. The total number of teachers and staff should be counted by individual people, and the duplicate number should be omitted. For example, if the total number of full-time male teachers is eight and the total number of part-time teachers is five, then the total number is thirteen. If the total number of full-time female teachers is twelve and the total number of part-time teachers is eight, then the total number is twenty. If the total number of full-time male staff is three and the total number of part-time staff is two, then the total number is five. If the total number of full-time female staff is six and the total number of part-time staff is four, then the total number is ten. If calculated according to the surface numbers, the total number of full-time male teachers and staff is eleven and the total number of part-time teachers and staff is seven, then the total number is eighteen. The total number of full-time female teachers and staff is eighteen and the total number of part-time teachers and staff is twelve, then the total number is thirty. The total number of full-time teachers and staff for men and women is twenty-nine, the number of part-time is nineteen, and the total number is forty-eight. However, upon investigation, the total number of male and female teachers and staff in the school can be 43. The error lies in the repeated appearance of part-time workers. Two of the five part-time male teachers are also staff at this school. Three of the four part-time female staff are also teachers at this school. A total of five people appear repeatedly and should be removed. Therefore, each row in this column should be filled in as follows: Male: 11 full-time, 5 part-time; Female: 18 full-time, 9 part-time; Total: 29 full-time, 14 part-time; Total: 43. At the same time, the explanation column should indicate that there are two male staff members who are also teachers at this school and three female staff members who are also teachers at this school. Not only does the total number conform, but the number of male and female teachers and staff who are also working outside the school can also be inferred.

10. The amount of annual income and expenditure is in yuan, and the amount below yuan is omitted. 11. The total amount should be the sum of the following items and must not have any discrepancies. 12. The total amount of annual income and expenditure must include both the regular and temporary expenses for the current year.

13. The annual income of public schools only has one item: public funds. Tuition is collected on behalf of the government and is not another kind of income other than public funds. It can be left blank to avoid confusion. However, private schools, or public schools where tuition is indeed the direct income of the school, should fill it in.

14. The experimental and practice supplies in the expenditure column include the costs of experiments in physics, chemistry, and biology, and the cost of practice in crafts.

15. Office and miscellaneous expenses include all office expenses, wages for laborers and workers, and various miscellaneous expenses. If the school has debts, the interest paid is also recorded in this item.

16. Construction refers to newly added buildings and civil engineering repairs of 500 yuan or more. Repairs below 500 yuan are included in the miscellaneous expenses item.

17. The amount of expenses per student is the quotient of the total number of students in the current year divided by the total amount of expenditure, with two decimal places below yuan.

18. In the establishment month and year column, record the month and year the school was established. For those established before the founding of the Republic of China, use the dating method before the era of recording years.

19. In the year and month of registration, record the year and month of the most recent registration. Public schools do not fill in this column.

20. In the principal column, fill in the name, background, and full-time or part-time status of the principal. If it is part-time, what other duties are held should be noted.

21. If the student and graduate columns cannot be filled in on one paper, two papers can be used. When using two papers, the items below the teacher column must be recorded on the second paper.

The First Day of the Chinese Economic Society's Annual Meeting

Forty Members Attend; Speeches by Shao Yuanchong and Others

Changes to the Annual Meeting's Order; Speeches by Dai Jitao and Others

Members Arrive in Wuxi: In the past two days, members from various regions have arrived in Wuxi, including Ma Yinchu (President) and his wife with Ms. Ni, Shao Yuanchong and his wife Zhang Mojun, Ma Chonggan and his wife (Head of Publicity), Chen Qicai, Chen Qixiong, Zhao Wenrui, Zhu Yangchen, Zhuang Zhihan, Hong Sibo (with family), Shi Weihuan (with family), Chen Zhenyi, Xu Zhaosun (with family), He Liang, Zhan Xianzhe, Shou Miancheng, Chen Can, Wang Shumei, Jiang Yuanxin, Han Zude, Liu Zhigan, Li Quanshi, Pan Xulun, Wang Zhenhan, Jiang Pingling, Jiang Chanshan, Zhou Zhongqian, Wei Songtang, Zhu Shikang, Xie Bingwen, Dai Ailu, Li Yunliang, and forty others.

The Situation During the Meeting: The meeting commenced at 9:00 AM yesterday (the 20th). All members were in attendance, with hundreds of guests arriving. After a collective bow and a moment of silence, President Ma Yinchu reported, with Xu Shi recording and Zou Tongyi as the master of ceremonies.

President Ma Yinchu's Report: President Ma Yinchu briefly described the society's history and stated that Wuxi is a region with developed industries and many entrepreneurs. Holding the annual meeting of economists here is quite appropriate. A fund of seventy thousand yuan has been raised. As for the quarterly journal, edited by Li Quanshi, three issues have already been published. The Zhejiang provincial government has agreed to lease the building on Baoshi Mountain to the society. After the report, Shao Yuanchong gave a speech. Mr. Shao's topic was "China's Economic Construction and Agricultural Policy," generally stating that those who desire a strong nation today include those who advocate for industry, those who advocate for agriculture, and those who advocate for other policies. However, industrial nations cannot abandon agricultural policies because agriculture is the foundation of industry. China has traditionally regarded agriculture as the foundation of the nation and possesses various virtues of farmers. Therefore, China's economic construction should focus on agricultural policy at present.

Dai Jitao's Speech: Due to a sudden outbreak of foot ailment at the Tangquan Hospital, Mr. Dai Jitao, a member of the Central Committee, was unable to attend Wuxi. He sent his speech to Wuxi via express mail, requesting Mr. Shi Weihuan to represent him in delivering the speech (the speech's length is omitted).

Visiting Various Factories: In the afternoon of the first day, the originally scheduled society affairs meeting was changed to factory visits, including visits to the Arts and Crafts Machinery Factory, Hengde Oil Factory, Qingfeng Yarn Factory, Lixin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, and Maoxin No. 2 Factory.

Pan Zhongjia's Banquet: Pan Zhongjia, the magistrate of Wuxi County, who is also a member of the society, hosted a banquet for all members and their families at the county chamber of commerce last night at 7:00 PM. Hosts and guests enjoyed themselves immensely before departing.

Changes to the Order: The order of the conference has been changed. The society affairs meeting originally scheduled for the afternoon of the 20th has been moved to the 22nd. A full day of sightseeing will take place on the 21st.

The First Committee Meeting of the People's Education Movement Commission

Decision to Start Pilot Programs in Hongkou and Zhabei

To promote popular education, the Shanghai YMCA has launched a People's Education Movement Organizing Committee, planning for all committee members to be respected figures in the education field, such as Wu Zhihui, Cai Zimin, Jiang Hongqi, Liu Zhan'en, Ou Yuanhuai, He Bingsong, Ge Gongzhen, Chuan Ruoyu, and twelve others. They convened the first committee meeting at noon yesterday at the YMCA, deciding to start pilot programs in Hongkou and Zhabei first. The first phase will enroll 1,000 male and female students, with courses including the "Common People's Thousand-Character Primer," phonetic symbols, and basic civic knowledge. The school locations are currently being discussed with various elementary schools and will be finalized soon. Enrollment is expected to begin on October 1st.

According to the Guowen News Agency, Japanese directors and committee members of the Shanghai Municipal Council (SMC), such as Murakami, have suggested to the SMC that new subsidies for the education of Japanese girls' schools and secondary schools be included in the next budget. The proposal was submitted for discussion at the SMC board meeting the other day, and all the directors expressed their support. A Chinese director present stated that Chinese directors have always advocated fairness and rejected bias in SMC administration. They expressed sympathy for the Japanese community's request for educational subsidies.

China Wins the Rober Cup Championship

Defeats England Yesterday by a Score of Three to One

6-8, 6-2, 6-2, 6-2

The International Rober Cup tennis tournament of the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Club had participants from China, England, Portugal, the United States, and Japan. China first defeated Japan, then the United States. England defeated Portugal, so China and England reached the finals. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, they competed for the final championship at the French Club. The Chinese representatives were Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai, and the English representatives were Whit and Stock. Four to five hundred spectators were present, making it a grand occasion. After a four-set battle, China won the championship with a score of 6-8, 6-2, 6-2, 6-2. The details are as follows.

A Brief History of the Rober Cup

The Rober Cup was established in 1921 to commemorate the late Mr. Rober. It was initially a doubles competition, with each country allowed to enter only one team. From 1912 to 1927, England won the championship four times and each other country had won it three times. Starting in 1928, it was officially changed to an international competition, and China joined that year, achieving good results. Portugal won two consecutive championships. This year, China sent Lin and Qiu to compete. The two players have outstanding skills and swept across Shanghai, invincible everywhere they went. Since their debut, they have repeatedly defeated strong opponents and won the championship, making history for the Chinese tennis community in Shanghai. This is truly something to celebrate.

The Skills of Both Sides

Yesterday's China-England final was a fierce competition. England's Whit is a veteran of the sea, and Stock is a rising star. They aimed to defeat Lin and Qiu to win the championship. They indeed won the first set with a score of 6-8. However, Lin and Qiu displayed the unpredictable skills of famous generals on the battlefield. After many wonderful points, they won the next three sets in a row, with the scores all being 6-2. This was truly remarkable. Lin Baohua's serving skills were excellent. In the four sets, he won as many as six games solely through his serves, which was commendable. Qiu Feihai showed some timidity, and his control was somewhat lacking. However, in the third and fourth sets, he regained his form, making rapid and decisive shots, earning the praise of the audience. England's Whit performed as usual, and Stock ran and covered a lot of ground, making great contributions. Stock's performance contributed significantly to England's results.

The Competitive Situation

First set, serving order: 1. Whit, 2. Lin Baohua, 3. Stock, 4. Qiu Feihai. England won the first game. Lin's serving with a slice won him a game. Then England added three games to make it 3-1. Lin and Qiu battled to a tie. England added two more games to make it 5-3. The Chinese team seemed to be in danger. Fortunately, they worked hard and were finally able to retaliate to tie the game at 5-5 (Lin won the tenth game with a slice). However, it was quite difficult. After that, it became 7-6. The Chinese team was still at a disadvantage. At that time, it was Lin Baohua's turn to serve, and it was thought that it would not be difficult to make it 7-7. Unexpectedly, Baohua, who is usually known for his fierce serves, had bad luck and could not fulfill his wish. England then won the first set 8-6 and got The Rober Cup Championship Left: Lin Baohua Right: Qiu Feihai (photographed by this newspaper)

Second set, serving order: 1. Stock, 2. Lin Baohua, 3. Whit, 4. Qiu Feihai. Lin and Qiu's sharpness gradually increased, and the situation turned around. They won four games in a row. Lin won a game with a slice. The English team tried hard to counterattack, winning two games. Lin and Qiu added two more games to win 6-2. The serving order for the third set was the same as the second. Qiu Feihai's shots were like arrows, repeatedly making great contributions. Lin Baohua's serves were like cannonballs, creating two more slices, robbing the English team, on the third game, making it a 5-1 lead, though the English tried and struggled, it was difficult to turn the tide, and so Lin and Qiu again winning with 6-2.

In the fourth set, Lin and Qiu lost fewer points, and the English team appeared scattered. Although they won the first game, they then lost five games in a row. At this point, the victory of the Chinese team was within their grasp. As a result, Lin and Qiu won again with 6-2, winning the Rober Cup.

Women's Singles Competition Not Held

After the group competition, there was originally a women's singles championship final. China's Li Xinghua lost to Martin in the semi-finals. Yesterday's final was supposed to be between Miss Fees and Martin. However, Miss Fees was unable to play due to illness, so it was canceled and will be held at a later date. At that time, China's Lin Baohua and England's Whit will play against China's Qiu Feihai and England's Stock in an exhibition doubles match. The enthusiasm for tennis is certainly high.

The Lawn Tennis Club's open doubles championship will be held at the French Club this afternoon starting at 3:00 PM. The order of the semifinals is as follows: 1. Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai vs. Canafan and Locola of Asia; 2. Shi Guia and Bude vs. Li De and Maida.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Hai Ke

Teacher (to a student): You've been studying for several years. How come you still can't write an essay well? Look at this commentary of yours. The writing has no brilliance, and the theory is very far-fetched.

Student: If I go home and tell my father this, won't he get angry?

Teacher: You just need to tell your father that you didn't do well this time and that you'll be more diligent in the future.

Student: That won't work. Because this essay was actually written entirely by my father for me.

A: Practicing the latest form of flexible gymnastics is the way to health. It can make the body healthy and extend life.

B: But there was no such thing as flexible gymnastics in ancient times. What about our ancestors?

A: That's why they're all dead now.

Music Student: Teacher, how do you think my voice sounds? Can it still be used?

Music Teacher: I think that if a fire were to break out in your house in the future, then your voice could be used to alert the neighbors.

Mother: Good child, don't help me anymore. Every time you help me, you always break one or two dishes.

Daughter: Mother, that's helping. If I break more dishes for you, then you can wash fewer next time.

Bo Baekke's Talk on Reforming China

— Jie Fei

Mr. Lin Baekke, the American legal advisor to the National Government, was a close friend of Dr. Sun Yat-sen before his death and a firm believer in the Three Principles of the People. He is planning to return to the United States to advocate for the abolition of unequal treaties for China and has many plans for the development of China's state-owned enterprises. Recently, he spoke about the reformation of China at the Central Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. His words were earnest and his good intentions are commendable. (The following is a record of Mr. Lin Baekke's words.)

The reformation of China requires the participation of foreigners, which has long been absolutely rejected by the United States. However, for the development of China's economy to be successful, it must rely on American assistance. Americans who have come to China have historically held two attitudes: malicious aggression and benevolent assistance. Missionaries belong to the former. I have severely criticized this point to the government. As for the second attitude, it is what I should do my best to support. For centuries, China has suffered from the aggression of the great powers, leading to this prolonged decline, unable to extricate itself from deep waters and scorching fires. Although it is China's illness, it is also the world's illness. The world is like a human body. If one organ is sick, the whole body will be affected. China's weakness is enough to cause instability in the world, so the great powers should assist China's development, which is also their duty. Considering today's great powers, only the United States can provide assistance in China's economic development. I am returning to my country this time to work hard on this matter. You are now students. Everyone has a responsibility for the development of China. You should prepare yourselves at this time to be loyal in the future. What you should pay attention to is being loyal to the country, loyal to the school, loyal to Mr. Sun Yat-sen, and to the Three Principles of the People he created, and even loyal to the principal of your school. If everyone is loyal, then China's prosperity can be expected soon, and unequal treaties can also be abolished without difficulty.

Jie An: Mr. Lin, as a foreigner, exhorts us to be loyal and use it as a tool for the future development of China. The people of the country should understand his satire and know what to be cautious about.

Talking about Jumping Jia Guan

— Tuo Gong

It is said that the theatrical performance of jumping Jia Guan is about Sun Shu Ao, the Chu prime minister in the Spring and Autumn Period. Meng learned that Shu Ao's son was poor, so he dressed in the prime minister's clothes and sang to enlighten the king. The world therefore associated it with him. I once heard from Historian Wang Zhixiang of Taicang that Jia Guan is a false official. Later generations harmonize the sound to flatter the rich and powerful. Liao Yingzhong's Jiangxing Miscellany says that actresses have a play of playing false officials. The one in green clothes holding a brief is called the Canjun Zhuang. This is proof of it. In ancient times, they wore green clothes, but now they wear red robes. The so-called holding a brief still remains the same today, that is, holding an ivory tablet on stage. Canjun Zhuang, or it is said that Zhuang is a borrowed word for dressing up. Also, Duan Anjie's Yuefu Miscellany says that during the Kaiyuan period, the actors Huang Fanchuo and Zhang Yefu played Canjun. It was already called Canjun in the Tang Dynasty. The historian also said that Mr. Wu Meicun's Yuanhu Song has a line that says "Snow-faced Canjun dances with starlings," which refers to jumping Jia Guan. The mask used by Jia Guan on stage today is as white as snow, so it is called snow-faced. Jia Guan is a common name, while Canjun is elegant. Dance is jumping. Wang Dao of the Jin Dynasty said to Xie Shang, "I heard that you can do the starling dance." The whole audience wanted to see it. Shang got up, put on his clothes and hat, and asked the audience to beat time. No one else mattered. The "dancing with starlings" mentioned in Mr. Meicun's poem is based on this. A guest asked me about the origin of jumping Jia Guan, so I recounted what I heard.

Obituary of Ms. Mao Jianpei

— Ji Cheng sent from the dove

Ms. Mao Jianpei suddenly passed away by poisoning. As a smart, capable, and enterprising young woman, her death has been mourned by all who knew her and those who did not. I knew Jianpei a few years ago. At that time, Jianpei's best friends, Ms. Ou Jingfen and Ms. Pei Fen, were also very close to Ms. Li Minghui. Minghui knew Jianpei through the two Ous, and I knew Jianpei through Minghui. At that time, Jianpei had not yet learned Peking opera, and she was not involved in the film industry. She was innocent, lively, and only sometimes talked about family problems. She often said that her father and mother were not on good terms, and her mother was a defenseless woman. I have to help my mother and fight for the family. In fact, Mao Yunke was very strict in managing the family. What Jianpei said may also be a one-sided view.

When Jianpei first entered the film industry, Yunke had no idea. When the film company signed a contract with Jianpei, she always told them to send a notice in advance of when and where the filming would take place. The car could wait beside the house. I will come out myself. There is no need to come in and urge me. She was afraid that her father would find out. Later, Yunke gradually heard about it. One morning, when Jianpei was going to the Kaiyuan Company to film the marriage contract, Yunke suddenly stopped her. There was a conflict between father and daughter. Jianpei then took her mother out and lived in a room in Anlegong. I went to comfort her at that time. Jianpei's younger brother, Yanqiu, and the two Ou sisters were also in the room. Jianpei said at the time that she could support her mother with her meager ability. If she was not allowed to make movies, she vowed not to go home. She was very angry. Later, Yunke was comforted by friends and gradually calmed down. Jianpei also followed the advice of her best friends and brought her mother back home. Then Yunke allowed his daughter to make movies, and the staff of the film company were able to enter and leave the Mao residence openly and aboveboard.

Yunke had no intention of letting Jianpei learn opera at first. After this incident, because his beloved daughter was interested in drama, he hired a teacher to teach her. Because Jianpei was so smart, she could learn quickly. After that, the father-daughter relationship gradually returned to its original state. When she performed on the big stage, the audience was packed for three days, and there was a continuous stream of applause. Yunke was still not satisfied, so he went north to study under Wang Yaoqing. Recently, he performed on the Hanzhao stage, and his reputation was soaring. Unexpectedly, she suddenly died. I know how painful the old father must be.

Jianpei was smart throughout her life, but she was always arrogant and refused to bow her head, which was her biggest problem. Now I hear that she died from taking medicine after arguing with a certain gentleman, then Jianpei's death was not from anything else, but from her lifelong problem.

It is heard that the film will be released on September 19th at the Paris Grand Theater. (Yun)

Acknowledgement: Zheng Jun Yimei is known for his miscellaneous works. He has long been famous in the north and south of the Yangtze River. Now, his masterpieces are compiled into a book called "Wanhua Jiaoxue Lu" and published by the Yixin Bookstore in Guomai. The entire book is more than 100,000 words long, and it is unique in its elegance. Yesterday, I received a copy, so I would like to express my gratitude here.

南洋游記（五五）

— 靈花

A Trip to the South Seas (55)

— Ling Hua

On the 21st, I took a public tram to the Kek Lok Si Temple. The city was hot and stuffy, and I wanted to study the social life of turtles. Along the way, the tram passed through coconut groves. I often saw the neat and tidy small plank houses of the Malay people. The coconut groves were covered with lush green vegetables. Such a new village would be very good if it were not subjected to capital suppression. Although the plank houses are small, they have phonographs. There are also Chinese houses. Although simple, the men and women who come out are neat and tidy. Only the women here are dyed in the Malay style, with thick powder on their faces, like whitewashed walls, like paintings, which is very inelegant and loses their original appearance. I arrived at the Kek Lok Si Temple to see the turtle pond under the pagoda. I paid close attention to the social life of the turtles. This turtle pond is about four or five zhang square. There are about a thousand turtles in it. The large ones can be three chi in diameter, and the small ones are only the size of an ordinary plate. Some are yellow, and some are white. They live very quietly. At 5 pm, the gardener put vegetable leaves in the water for them to eat. When they saw the vegetable leaves, they all raised their heads and came forward, as if being called by name. Some quietly lay beside the stones and did not come. They are hermits. They compete for the vegetable food, but not fiercely. Whoever gets it is their fate. The power of pushing and shoving is very weak. It is rare to see them biting each other like a pack of dogs. I asked someone who had lived here for a long time whether turtles fight. He said he had never seen it. I think this creature is very noble and quiet. Their society is not governed but not chaotic. Therefore, Fu Xi drew the eight trigrams according to the patterns on turtle shells, and all philosophy comes from the I Ching. Therefore, the sacred turtle is the ancestor of Eastern culture. Later generations, Yang Xiong, imitated the I Ching to write the Tai Xuan. Sima Guang spent thirty years annotating it. And Ziyun, in his "Explanation of Ridicule," said to his guests, "Now you ridicule the turtle dragon with a gecko, and you are claiming to be a turtle." In the Han Dynasty, there was the musician Li Guinian, in the Tang Dynasty, there was the literary man Lu Guimeng, and in the Song Dynasty, there was the Confucian scholar Yang Guishan. Today, many Japanese people have turtles as their surnames, such as Kamezawa Taro, Jiro, etc. Alas, the turtle society is a society of few desires and no contention, a society of perfect governance.

I also tried hard to observe whether the big turtles bullied the small turtles. Sometimes the small turtles crossed over the big turtles, and the big turtles did not care. It was like what I saw in Taiyuan. The cattle were eating grass, and flocks of birds flew onto the backs of the cattle. Flocks of birds also came to the troughs and ate with the cattle. The cattle did not hate them at all. There was also a hen raised in the Taiyuan Museum. It lived alone in a wooden house. The house had an inner and outer room. Its food was stored in the inner room. Many small sparrows came from outside. They entered its inner room and ate. They entered and exited from under the chicken's wings. The chicken did not care. The concept of ownership of cattle and chickens is so weak. Therefore, there is no need for legislators to stipulate hundreds of articles. If human morality were like that of birds and beasts...

心上温馨（二八一）

— 包天笑

Heart's Warmth (281)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboo Tears Stain Her Face, Broken Heart / Red Lotus Fragrance Fades, A Maiden Soul Departs

This interrogation proved that everything he said was lies. But without real evidence, it was impossible to make a judgment at the time. But investigation was inevitable. Those detectives were even more厲害 than Sherlock Holmes of England. In just a few days, they had found out all his movements. But this wife was not the formal wife of Zhang Yiqing after all. She could not put on the airs of a principal wife. Only in her own house was her sovereignty absolute. She racked her brains on the opium couch. Thinking that Zhang Yiqing was so unfaithful, it was really hateful. She couldn't wait to make a big fuss with him. She had to tell the person he brought from outside to get the hell out. But on second thought, she couldn't act rashly. The current Zhang Yiqing was someone who could move on his own. He was not like before, when he was immobile and dependent on her. If she made too much noise and he couldn't turn around, she would suffer instead. People say that a cornered dog will jump over the wall. If he turned his face and said you are not my wife, it is none of your business, and kicked me over, I would not be able to settle this account with him. But making a fuss about it would not be fun. She had to think of another way. It was better to use soft methods than hard ones, subtle methods than crude ones. She would slowly clean them up. So she used methods to deceive him step by step, using sweet words to please him. When he said he was going on a boat ten days into this month, she still let him go. But she made it clear that the family already knew that he was not going on a boat. And she already knew where his small mansion was. Sometimes, she deliberately mentioned it in her words. Zhang Yiqing wanted to cover it up, but he could not. One day, she formally opened negotiations with Zhang Yiqing. She said, "I have known for a long time that you have someone outside. You don't need to hide it from me. A man is not forbidden to have three wives and four concubines as long as he can afford it. I only hope that you don't forget the old for the new. That would be good." Zhang Yiqing listened to her words, which sounded very pitiful, so he didn't say anything. Not saying anything was like tacitly acknowledging it. That wife continued, "Moreover, I am not your formal wife. I can't interfere with you. But because we used to be comrades in distress, I helped you. Now you men are nothing. We women are finished for life. Our reputations are ruined. We have no face to see the dead on the road to the underworld." Saying that, she lay on the pillow and sobbed. Women's tears are enough to melt a man's heart. After Zhang Yiqing took Cuiyun, he was prepared to break up with that unofficial wife if she made a lot of noise. He didn't expect her to use soft methods instead of hard ones.

滬金融界之特殊狀

Special Situation in the Shanghai Financial World

時局進展洋用甚廣厘價奇漲

The Situation is Developing, and the Use of Foreign Silver is Very Extensive, and the Cent Price is Rising Sharply

滬埠金融界最近因前方戰事勝利彼此額手稱慶對於各種投機及投資營業作熱烈之競爭引起市面之特殊變動外滙步長標金平謐而超下各種證劵公債相將上俏買户擁擠需用洋欵尤爲殷繁更以銀行大舉購買洋欵備作種種流動運用之籌碼故洋厘被各方而激動近日亦隨之狂抬奇漲而軍需每日裝出甚多致金融市面特變據金融界方面推測證劵之漲風正未有艾而洋厘之加昻固意中事如再經外埠各處需洋要求則滬埠現洋價恐有繼抬之虞

Recently, the financial community in Shanghai has been celebrating the victory in the front-line battles and has been engaged in fierce competition for various speculative and investment operations, which has caused special changes in the market. Foreign exchange is increasing, gold is stable, and various securities and government bonds are rising sharply. Buyers are crowded, and the demand for foreign silver is particularly strong. The banks are buying foreign silver in large quantities to prepare for various liquid uses. Therefore, the foreign silver cent is being stimulated by all parties, and it has also been rising sharply recently. The military supplies are being loaded out in large quantities every day, which has caused special changes in the financial market. According to the speculation of the financial community, the rising trend of securities is not over, and the increase in the price of foreign silver cents is intentional. If there is a demand for foreign silver in various places outside the port, the price of current foreign silver in Shanghai may continue to rise.
