Grain and Rice Market's Declining Trend Intensifies

Early New Japonica Rice Falls More Than Half a Yuan

Late New Japonica Rice Falls Half a Yuan to One Yuan

New Xiang Rice Falls Slightly More Than One Yuan

Yesterday at Zhabei, a total of thirty ships arrived from various routes. Although buying interest was strong, the consensus was bearish. Consequently, even with reduced supplies of early Japonica rice, prices still declined. The arrival of late Japonica rice has not been substantial recently. However, market sentiment turned bearish due to clear weather, leading to a sharp decline. Top-quality rice saw a price decrease of twenty to thirty cents, while mid-grade rice fell by more than half a yuan. Exceptional quality rice barely reached twenty yuan and twenty-three cents. The supply of early Japonica rice was limited. However, factories still held inventory, so once it was released, the market price struggled to hold, and prices dropped sharply by a little over one yuan to half a yuan, with prices hovering between nineteen yuan and a half to nineteen yuan. The arrival of new Xiang rice has been plentiful, but sales have been slow. The price has also dropped sharply by sixty to seventy cents. Mid- to low-grade rice must sell for a little over one yuan less. Top-grade rice is only offered at fourteen yuan and forty or fifty cents, while mid- to low-grade rice is only thirteen yuan and ten or twenty cents. The trend for new Du Zi Xiang rice and new Jiao Bai Xiang rice is also softening, with the overall market falling by thirty to forty cents. The decline in new Ke Jian rice is particularly steep due to continuous arrivals from Ningbo and cautious retail sales, causing the market to plummet without a standard price, generally around thirteen yuan, with very few transactions. The new Bu Jian market has also fallen by about forty cents, with top-quality rice already dropping into the fourteen yuan range. Conditions within the customs area remain stable. The overall market has neither gains nor losses. The market shape for new Japonica and Xiang rice for the whole day has shown a sharp downward turn. Old stocks will also follow the downward trend soon.

The supply from South Shanghai and He Xia is limited, and sales are sluggish. Broken white rice is sold as soon as it arrives, showing a steady trend. Sales of the South Shanghai Bo Dao rice are quiet, with prices between twenty yuan and seventy or eighty cents for high-quality rice. The arrival of new Japonica rice here is very scarce, and the price has fallen back in line with the northern market. Fragrant Japonica rice has also fallen by a little over twenty cents, with high-quality rice offered at twenty yuan. The selling of new Yang Jian rice is becoming brisker, and sellers are eager to sell. New Jian rice is also weak and sluggish. The arrival of Du Zi Jian rice is also being met with a very soft market. Overall, the price of each Jian rice has fallen by about thirty cents, with the situation showing a tendency to decline further.

Foreign Rice Origin Prices Reported Down by Three to Four Cents

Jiangxi Rice Also Drops by Two and a Half Cents

Yesterday, prices at the origin of foreign rice were reported down by three to four cents. Many foreign firms in the market are peddling Saigon rice. Besides Saigon, various ports in Burma also reported slight decreases. Small batches of first and second month Xiaoxiao rice are priced at six liang and one qian, while the Saigon rice currently being loaded is priced at seven liang and two or three qian, consistent with early market prices. However, Shanghai merchants are seeing new rice entering the market daily, with news of abundant harvests from various regions. Although foreign rice is cheap and profitable, they are afraid of repeating past mistakes and dare not place orders.

Yesterday, over five thousand bags of new Jiangxi rice arrived, with more expected to arrive continuously. However, sales in Shanghai have stalled, with limited buying interest on this street. The consensus is bearish, and the market immediately shows a downward trend, falling by as much as two and a half cents compared to the previous day. It is estimated that six hundred bags of Jiangxi rice were procured early by this street's brokers at a price of twelve yuan and ten and a half cents to eleven yuan and eighty cents; three hundred bags later at sixteen yuan and ten cents; and two hundred bags of the original price at seventeen yuan and a half.

Marked Flour Market Opens Strong and Rises

Flour Transportation Ban Lifted, Filling Speculative Short Positions

Yesterday, after the morning and afternoon opening of the flour market, prices for each month rose step by step. Although the price of foreign wheat continued to decrease by four, five, six, or seven cents, the current situation has turned optimistic, and the flour transportation ban has indeed been lifted. Although this year's northern harvest is abundant, southern flour has been unavailable for a long time. Realistically speaking, there will eventually be a greater need. Since the political situation and the transportation ban have been resolved simultaneously, market sentiment will inevitably become enthusiastic. Therefore, buying interest in each session of the morning and afternoon has been strong. Speculative short positions outside the industry are also being covered substantially at any time. As a result, near-term and distant terms have become more expensive based on actual sales and disregard the price of foreign wheat. As a result, this month has risen two cents and seven and a half mils compared to the previous day, October has risen two and a half cents, November has risen two cents, December and January have risen half a cent, and February has risen one cent and seven and a half mils.

Wheat Market Shows Signs of Weakness

Yesterday, after the morning and afternoon opening of the wheat market, prices for each month suddenly turned up and became firm. Because the current situation is improving, it is expected that future flour sales will change from stagnant to smooth, so the future of wheat naturally also has hope. Although foreign wheat is still reported down, the current must ultimately take into account actual sales. The ratio of foreign countries seems to have an emergency that is far from enough. The gradual rebound in market conditions is not without reason. As a result, September and October rose by four cents compared to the previous day, November rose by five cents, and December to February rose by four cents. The market condition of spot wheat has stabilized for exceptionally high-quality wheat. However, mid- and low-quality wheat have thick inventories on the market. Customers see that the factory's demand has been activated, and they are all seeking to sell first, so each grade is slightly lower by two or three cents. However, the northern transport after a smooth journey should not be smaller. More than 10,000 packages of Shandong red and white wheat, Yaowan wheat, and Bao Ying Sha Shi wheat were opened and went to Fuxin to select the high-quality ones, and 5,700 packages were taken away.

North and South Goods, Candied Date Market Trends Toward Stability

Candied dates have recently been arriving successively, and the market is gradually stabilizing. Sales are still good. Yesterday, Huigong Tutu sold twenty-six liang of Jiaxing goods, and Tutu sold twenty-two or twenty-three liang. The upper and lower grades still follow the previous example with an added discount. The top large-grained "Super Egg" dates sold for as high as thirty liang. There is also a type made from apples that is as crystal clear as dates and sells for seventy yuan, but the output is very small.

Piece Goods: Northern Merchants Search for Eastern Fabrics

The piece goods market has rebounded and is trending higher. Northern merchants are searching for Eastern goods very eagerly. Because the situation is deteriorating rapidly, Osaka's fixed prices have soared. Therefore, merchants from Tianjin and Qingdao are coming to Shanghai to search for spot goods. Yesterday, the most traded goods were fine serge, with two to three hundred pieces traded. 球 has sold for three qian, one fen and a half, Huxinting is sold at two qian and seven fen, and Hanshan, etc., at two qian, six fen and seven li. This is two li and a half higher than the highest market price last week. Local merchants see customer help activities and are also moving forward one after another. Yuehua velvet has risen back to the highest price previously opened. Large-patterned and mid-patterned are already two qian, and black flower is one qian, nine fen and two and a half mils. Direct tribute woolen cloth, with the hardest body above the middle grade, has been out of stock for a while, and Santan Yin Yue has already been transported and opened at three qian and four fen, Shile black at three qian and four and a half fen, and Lie Yan at three qian, one fen and a half. Moganshan is at three qian, one fen and two and a half mils. In addition to this street, Han merchants also need a lot. The Ting Nei, which has a deep flower color, has also been popular recently, having risen from two qian to two qian and five mils. Western goods are still stagnant. Only Sichuan merchants have released more than one hundred pieces of Fang Li direct tribute woolen cloth in recent days, with a price of two qian and four fen.

Light Fabrics and Woolens Selling Briskly in a Timely Manner

Sales Prices Rising Due to Lack of Goods

Recently, light fabrics such as 嗶叽, serge, patterned woolens, direct tribute velvet, and chocolate woolen cloth from the woolen guild have been selling very well. Local merchants have healthy demand. Patterned woolens with new designs are popular. 嗶叽拆藍 must be matched with other colors of Huate woolens, only navy blue is more expensive, because most of them are needed for Western clothes. Plaid-colored Huate woolens also sell quite well. The trend for hat woolens is also good. The sales price continues to rise because there is a lack of arriving stock.

Hardware: English White Iron, Thick Patterns and Colors Scarce

Recently, there has been a shortage of English white iron with thick patterns and colors in circulation. Because the previous month's prior order fell sharply, hardware industry suffered a lot, so they are reluctant to place orders, so it has been a long time since no orders have been placed. Because there are not many goods currently arriving, the standard price is soaring. At the moment, the estimated price for No. 34 is twelve liang and a half per box, No. 26 is fourteen liang, No. 28 is fourteen liang and seven qian and a half, and No. 31 is sixteen liang and two qian and a half, which is two qian and a half higher than the previous day.

Coal Market: Small Decline Expected in Gold Prices in the Coal Market

Foreign Firm Orders Have Not Arrived, and There is Also a Shortage

At the moment, the gold price is fluctuating. All dealers are expecting a small decline in its price. For the time being, no foreign firm orders have been made. The number of current arrivals is also small, and sales are also very sluggish. Yesterday at the tea party, the main merchants' transactions amounted to more than two hundred tons of white coal and seven hundred tons of bituminous coal. The market is stable.

Business News

Pathe Company of Sichuan Road declares that the company has produced thousands of records over the years, which are sold all over the world and are very popular. Last month, more than 20 new records were released. Diamond needles and steel needles follow the convenience of customers. These records are the first batch of products recorded by the company from the United States last year with newly purchased radios. The results are very good, so they are selling like hotcakes since they were released. In particular, the most famous performers, Yunlu Jushi's Wupen Ji, Feng Zhaoliang's Wujiapo Qingyi, and the famous actors Li Jiri, Chen Shanfu, Xu Biyun, Rong Lijuan, Cao Mingsanhong, have sold the most. The sales offices in this area and other areas are very busy, it is said.

Bede Company, No. 91 Sichuan Road, declares that the company's retail department has launched a butterfly-style Broadway collar flower style, which is very beautiful and is the most fashionable. Major stores in this area and other areas have been ordering them enthusiastically, and the retail sales in the retail department are also quite a lot every day.

Yusheng Silk Weaving Factory declares that the factory is located in Tianbao Road and Tiande Road. It specializes in manufacturing different kinds of silks and satins with the latest electric motors. The prices are low and the products are excellent. Recently, in order to expand its business, in addition to setting up a general distribution office in Taozhuli, Erli Road, this area, a second distribution office has now been set up at No. 60 Sanma Road for wholesale and retail, and a retail department has also been set up in the National Products Market.

Taicang Food Company of Nanjing Road declares that the company is scheduled to start a big price reduction for two weeks from September 22nd. All goods will be sold at 65% to 90% of the marked price. All kinds of moon cakes are of excellent color, aroma and taste, with cheap prices and good quality. The people of Shanghai are really lucky.

Huachanglong, Zhongmantingfangkou, Five Ma Road, declares that the store has been established for six years, and its prosperity is rare. Now, on the occasion of the anniversary, it has specially prepared a large number of domestic silks and satins, Guangdong woolen cloth, woolen cloth, serge, Shunquanlong umbrellas, and various silk fabrics, all of which are beautifully prepared to meet the needs of all walks of life. It also reduces prices and sells them at a loss for 30 days to thank customers for their kind intentions. The people who have been purchasing in recent days are unusually crowded, and the threshold is almost broken, causing the road to be blocked.

Theater News

The Star Film Company announces that their film "Peach Blossom Lake," recently assembled with abundant film talent and produced on a large scale, has now been fully completed after more than two months. A private screening was held yesterday, and the company is confident that the performances of Hu Die, Zheng Xiaoqiu, Xia Peizhen, etc., are profound.

Director Zheng Zhengqiu's directorial skill is meticulous, the scenery is rich and magnificent, and the lighting is soft and pleasing. In every aspect, it is comparable to the company's previous blockbusters such as "Plum Blossom Falls," "Orchid in the Empty Valley," and "White Cloud Pagoda," and the emotional impact is even greater than these films. It is said that it will be released publicly in Shanghai on Double Ten Day. At that time, it is expected that the festive season and the excellent film will create a grand occasion.

The World Grand Theater, located at the corner of Baoxing Road and Qingyun Road in Zhabei, announces that since the other day, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters issued a notice that soldiers watching movies must purchase tickets. A platoon of soldiers is specially assigned to the theater every day to maintain order, which is very peaceful. Starting today, the theater will show the latest great production of the Star Film Company, the thirteen-episode "Burning the Red Lotus Temple." The film has a precise structure, magnificent scenery, and unique illusions. Director Zhang Shichuan's direction is skillful, and the performances of Hu Die, Xia Peizhen, and Zhou Wenzhu in this film are particularly earnest, making it even more exciting and worth watching than the previous episodes.

The Wuchang Grand Theater announces that starting today, the theater will screen "Hu Tune Woman," starring the exceptionally skilled and famous actress Fan Mingke Pipa Taniell. The plot of the film is tortuous and extremely humorous, and the performance of the comedy star Lei Meng Ge Laifeishi adds to its splendor. The film will be screened continuously for four days at the theater starting today, and free cigarettes will still be given away.

Shen Bao Pictorial Weekly

(1) The China National Aviation Corporation's amphibious aircraft "Jiujiang" took off from the Longhua seaplane airport at 8:15 am on September 12th for a test flight to Chongqing. It is reported that the trip went smoothly and official service is expected to begin next month, with weekly round trips. The 3,600-mile long trip will take only 12 hours if there are no stops along the way.

— (W)

(2) The "Jiujiang" aircraft arrived at Wangjiadun Airport in Hankou at 3:05 pm on the same day. The photo shows, from left to right, the pilot Mr. Smith, the assistant manager of China National Aviation Corporation Mr. Hamilton, the head of the flight crew Mr. Nie Kaiyi, and the mechanic Mr. Bian Zugen.

— (Qixin, Hankou)

(3) The North Sichuan Railway to Chongqing is not far away. It starts from the east bank of the Jialing River in Jiangbei County, passes along Mount Hua, and ends at the west bank of Hechuan County, a distance of 120 li. It was initiated by Mr. Li Chougen and Mr. Tang Jianzhang, who raised 300,000 yuan to form a company. Construction of the section from the Jialing River bank to Wenxingchang was started in the autumn of the 17th year of the Republic and is now nearing completion. The railway is mainly used for transporting coal and also for transporting passengers. The northeast is mostly mountainous, making it difficult to lay railway tracks. After the failure of the Sichuan-Han Railway Company, entrepreneurs have regarded it as a long journey. However, the colleagues of the North Sichuan Company did not avoid difficulties and completed it to the end. Those who are enthusiastic about entrepreneurial endeavors can see that the country can rise up from this.

(4) A group photo of the members of the Guangdong-Yunnan and Hunan-Yunnan railway surveying teams of the Ministry of Railways visiting the Bronze Temple (also known as the Golden Temple) in Yunnan.

(5) The Luoping County Waterfall in Yunnan is about 120 feet high and about 200 feet wide, with a horsepower of about 300,000. It is only 20 li away from the Guangdong-Yunnan railway line and can be used as a source of power for developing industries and driving vehicles in the future.

(6) A group photo of the Chairman of the Guizhou Provincial Government, Mr. Mao Guangxiang, and representatives of various institutions welcoming the Guangdong-Yunnan and Hunan-Yunnan railway surveying teams.

(7) The Huangguoshu Waterfall in Guizhou is located at the junction of Zhenning and Guanling counties and is located upstream of the Baishui River. It is about 350 feet high and about 150 feet wide. The provincial government is currently planning to use this water to generate electricity to develop industries.

A Journey to Dante's Hometown

— Hualin

(Artistic World) and (Scientific World) are the crystallization of human culture. One belongs to the expression of inner life, is subjective, imaginative, and transcends all interests, so that we do not fall into the bitterness of reality but appreciate all the beauty of life, with hope and passion, so living science is art, making our lives richer and striving for the path of creation. The other belongs to the exploration of the external world, is objective, rational, analyzes all phenomena, and seeks a kind of equivalent explanation, but based on the established facts, it is the result of the facts rather than the origin of the facts, so dead art is science, and it can provide us with many lessons, making our power to invade the external world more precise and changing the grand view of the world. These two often conflict. One seeks the absolute sublime beauty, and the other seeks a relative analysis of the truth. In fact, life is all in these (two worlds). The true literary artist is not just a daydream, a frenzy, but also puts it into practice, leading the masses to the path of light, creating an ideal new kingdom in this melancholy and dark world, so the artist's mind is never bound by reality, his heart is in the famous mountains, in the peaks, and friends with the colorful clouds, and friends with the stars and moon. He hates all achievements and despises all mediocrities, but he is also a prophet, seeing the justice that people do not see and loving the greatness that people do not feel. This kind of (passion) abandons everything in the world, but everything belongs to him. I am convinced that the greatness of this kind of personality is definitely not something that the scientific world can imagine. I traveled to Italy to explore the secret of the Renaissance and felt a profound lesson in life. Please say a word to the famous city (Florence) first.

In the dark ages of the Middle Ages, the Papal Party and the Royalist Party fought each other, foreign troubles arose frequently, and internal worries followed. Mediocre people tended to curry favor, and virtuous people lived and died in exile. The heroes who reformed politics and religion were burned to death in front of the Old Palace. The poets who rushed to save their country could not be tolerated in their hometowns, and the architects, sculptors, and painters starved to death on the poor roads and were exiled in foreign countries. In more than 1,300 years, most of the city was destroyed by fire, the Black and White parties fought for power, there was a great flood and a terrifying plague, and the Papal Party and the Royalist Party fought more cruelly. Unexpectedly, a ray of light was found in this dark world, that is, the literary artists confronted reality and declared war on power. They created many models of great personalities in their fantasies, and they broke through the prison of selfishness and self-interest in their passion. A fierce war left many traces. Hundreds of years later, the light shone everywhere. Who would dare to say that modern culture was not influenced by the Renaissance, and who would not say that (Dante's Divine Comedy) was the only guide to indicate light in the darkness? Like China's (Qu Yuan, our close friend, the world will be split in half, no matter where you go, it is only the (Qu Yuan world) and the (non-Qu Yuan world) (Dante) is a latecomer in the Qu Yuan world. When I was in (Florence), I admired the works of many artists, the first of which was (Giotto), the creator of Dante's friend. He and the three words (Dante) (Florence) are intertwined. (Giotto) is an architect, a sculptor, and a painter. He is a good friend of (Dante) (Bettia Ge). In all of his creations, he only expresses the highest passion and love. Others, such as the sculptor (Donatello), express the effort of life, and the frescoes of (Ang Eli Guo) are intoxicatingly elegant and mysterious. But every time I visit the tomb of (Medici) and appreciate (Michelangelo's) four statues, I become the reincarnation of life day and night, expressing the extremely tired life with extremely powerful muscles. There is also a statue of a thinker, which and (Vinci's) (Smile) become the eternal mystery of life, which no one can guess. This statue is the statue of (Medici Ronhang), a thinker wearing a warrior's costume, but his face is hidden in the crown, and his posture does not have a clear indication. There are two statues in this hall, one representing a dreamer and the other representing a businessman, but they are all powerful warriors in the bitterness of day and night. This mystery cannot be guessed to the end. Human beings are all working hard in this way to go to (Florence), the genius of (Wen Si) is the (Savior) painted, what a profound expression of the power of the world, the tragic fate of life is sacrificed because of love, and the extremely simple curve expresses the extremely compassionate passion. For such masterpieces, it can be seen how deeply literary artists penetrate into the inner heart of life, and the lesson they give us is only to constantly strive to die for love! (Vinci) is an uninhibited genius, a literary artist and a scientist, who died in France, just like the poet (Bettia Ge) who wandered in France and admired a woman named (Lao), whom he praised for the rest of his life. They both felt the unfortunate fate of their motherland and could not be known at that time, which shows that the more genius is tempered, the greater the power of creation will be. Don't you see that (Masaccio), who starved to death in a humble room, left behind immortal masterpieces, completed (Giotto's) soul in the (Ge Mai) Church in Florence, and attached it with a physical creation, surpassing his predecessors in precision, but his life was poor, which is probably the reason why heaven bestowed genius. It shows that (cultivating genius is passion, not wealth, and what we demand to be satisfied is desire, not selfishness). Only by understanding this can we understand the value of life and do a great unworthy undertaking instead of ordinary people, who are constantly immersed in selfishness and do not know that there are shameful things in the world. I traveled to (Athens) in Italy and heard the wind of (Plato) in the countryside, drank the spring of love of (Dante), sang in front of (Lily), lingered on the banks of the (Arno) River, which made my heart drunk and my love infatuated. I only know that (the need for mood) is far better than hunger and cold. Whether it is a literary artist or a scientist, only (love) can increase the happiness of life. What I call happiness is that it cannot be found in dreams and cannot be obtained in the real world. In other words, only a person with great ambition, only a person with great passion, can despise all wealth and power and create a new civilization of splendor for the world. Now (Florence) is left with traces of blood, which is wet, I don't know, but what the genius demands for his personal satisfaction is all the more terrifying and makes people bow down, that is (creating a new world for love and destroying an old world for hate).
